  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer13795479652578333076"><b>
  <i>Long live the King... </i>
</b><br/><br/>After turning his back on the throne for centuries, Wrath, son of Wrath, finally assumed his father’s mantle—with the help of his beloved mate. But the crown sets heavily on his head. As the war with the Lessening Society rages on, and the threat from the Band of Bastards truly hits home, he is forced to make choices that put everything—and everyo</span>
  <span id="freeText13795479652578333076" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Long live the King... </i>
</b><br /><br />After turning his back on the throne for centuries, Wrath, son of Wrath, finally assumed his father’s mantle—with the help of his beloved mate. But the crown sets heavily on his head. As the war with the Lessening Society rages on, and the threat from the Band of Bastards truly hits home, he is forced to make choices that put everything—and everyone—at risk.<br /><br />Beth Randall thought she knew what she was getting into when she mated the last pure blooded vampire on the planet: An easy ride was not it. But when she decides she wants a child, she’s unprepared for Wrath’s response—or the distance it creates between them.<br /><br />The question is, will true love win out... or tortured legacy take over?</span>
  <a data-text-id="13795479652578333076" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I don't think so Harriette. I haven't read this one yet but I have read all the others and even though the author might repeat what happened previousl<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I don't think so Harriette. I haven't read this one yet but I have read all the others and even though the author might repeat what happened previously I think there would be too much detail and events for you to keep track and read it enjoyably. Each book follows a different couple and this one continues the story of the couple in the very first book <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42899.Dark_Lover">https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4...</a> . I would recommend you read the first book either way,it's a pretty good series.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

  <span id="freeText12866474641458311495" style="display:none">Hey, I just thought of something . . .<br><br><b>WHEN BETH GOES INTO HER NEEDING QHUINN AND BLAY WILL BE GOING AT IT LIKE RABBITS FOR HOURS ON END</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793696i/581574.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*passes out*<br>________________________________________<br><br><b>Scroll down for exciting news on the future of the BDB series, tidbits about the Fallen Angels series, and info on the next book. But be warned: there are spoilers if you've not finished reading Lover At Last.</b><br><br><br><b>&gt;</b>The next book is about Wrath and Beth and is titled <i>The King</i>; it will be about him having an heir.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>We will see more of Murdher in the future books, but something needs to happen with Xhex before Murdher will get his own book; more on that when the timing is right.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Saxton – Big keep reading!<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>About Rhage and Mary’s novella: Ward is about 146 pages in, now she only needs to finish it.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>The next Fallen Angels book is titled <i>Possession</i> and the cover was shown at the event. (I am guessing it will be only soon too, then?)<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Lassiter will get a book when he’s ready – he opens up a whole storyline and she’s not sure whether he’ll feature in BDB or Fallen Angels (she didn’t not say both ;) ) <br><br><b>&gt;</b>What about movies? She’s focused on the books but said that could only happen with someone who could do the books justice.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>She doesn’t know how Layla’s pregnancy will go – another KEEP READING! However, she <i>did</i> say that Layla's pregnancy will take a long time since she is a pure bred, but Beth’s pregnancy may be more in line with humans since she is a half breed.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Lash WILL be back, she just doesn’t know when.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Is there a connection between Michael (Story of Son) and Murdher – answer “Duh!” but doesn’t know if it will be “seen” in a book.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Sola isn’t related to Manny and Butch.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>How will it work with Qhuinn and Blay, Layla, Xcor and the baby – KEEEEEP REEEADING!!<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Did the Scribe Virgin create the Shadows – they are a subspecies that developed on their own.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>In regard to Assail – Warden thinks he’s awesome, she’s obsessed with him and his cousins are totally effin HOT!!<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>There is a nexus with the Fallen Angels battle for good and the development of the BDB plotline – she thinks it could go either way but a crossover is logical.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>There wasn’t anything else (or anyone else) in the barrels with Luchas. <br><br><b>&gt;</b>Qhuinn and Luchas return to their parent’s house, Qhuinn sees Luchas as a victim and we’ll see more of Luchas in future books.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will we find out more about the glymera female who had an orgy with the Bastards – yes! She also hosted that dinner with Wrath . . . she is married to the really old guy.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Why didn’t we get Ehric’s twin’s name – because she writes what she sees and doesn’t know it yet.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Are Sissy and Jim going to fall in love – KEEEEEEEEEEEEEEP REEEEEEEEEADING!!<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will Nalla have a book so we can see Zsadist lose his sh!t? She doesn’t know yet.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will Xcor turn on the Bastards for Layla – KEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEP REEEEEEEEEEEADING!!!<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will we find out about Butch and Manny’s father and if there are more kids – KEEEEEEEEEEEEEP REEEEEEEEEEEEEEEADING!!<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Layla is considered Fallen (Chosen, not angel ;) )<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will Butch be in another book? Yes, and we’ll see some closure for him and José.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Are they going to expand the rules for brotherhood inductions? Yes and Blay, Payne and Xhex could be inducted in future.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Were there a lot of edits for the Blay and Qhuinn sex scenes? – There was nothing edited out.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Payne can help heal the Brothers of injuries etc but she doesn’t know if Payne’s gift is with limits or has to be replenished but she WILL keep George alive (as in longer than reg dogs ;) ) <br><br><b>&gt;</b>No definite plans for a second Insiders’ Guide buuuuuuuut maybe in the future.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will the Sribe Virgin be in <i>The King</i>? She doesn’t know but something will need to be done with her.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Wrath still owes the Scribe Virgin that favor . . .<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>There WILL be more about Jane and V – she’s also talking to her publisher about revisiting each couple in full book form. (HELL YES!!!)<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Do we know who Elan was talking to? ANSWER: Yes - SAXTON’S FATHER!!!!!<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will any major character die? KEEEEEEEEEEEEP REEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEADING!!!<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Both Blay and Qhuinn release bonding scents(!)<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Is Saxton working on the full blooded heir law? Not yet.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Are Tohr and Xcor brothers? She's not saying a thing . . . (My guess is yes, and that will be Xcor's saving grace.)<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will there be two males bonded to one female – again she ain’t talking.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Are Throe’s family alive and in/be in the books? KEEEEEEEEEEEEEP REEEEEEEEEEEEEEADING!!!!<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will Fritz get a story – she doesn’t think he can be developed into a story.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will Havers ever be redeemed and have a story? NO!!!<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will Havers be in <i>The King</i> and deliver Wrath and Beth’s baby – KEEP READING (but over the WARDen’s dead body!!!)<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Is Sola human? 100%, absolutely human.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Is Xhex living in the mansion with John Matthew? Yep, they have worked through their issues :D<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Will we see Layla’s baby soon? Yes.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Do we know about the coffins in the garage? Not yet but she *thinks* it may come up in <i>The King</i>.<br><br><b>&gt;</b>Is Phury going to do better by the Chosen? KEEEEEEEEEEEEEP REEEEEEEEEEEEEADING!!<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>Is Eddie coming back? We’ll see him buuuuuuuuuuut KEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEP REEEEADING!!!<br><br><b>&gt;</b>Phury’s future is tied up with the Scribe Virgin.<br><br><b>&gt;</b>Saxton will play a major part in an upcoming plot line.<br> <br><b>&gt;</b>And, lastly, Qhuinn and Blay will be mated (as in, the whole ceremony with the carving of the names in each of their backs, true?). (Again, HELL YES!!!)</span>

<div id="review_646581999" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/646581999" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/646581999?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11963959-lisa?shelf=love-you-forever-and-ever">love-you-forever-and-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11963959-lisa?shelf=favourite-series">favourite-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646581999" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9792131685720515666"><b>FIVE ALL HAIL THE KING STARS.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396596046i/9157790._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396596046i/9157791._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>JR Ward has not failed me yet, this series is nothing short of phenomenal and I don't ever want to stop reading about this band of brothers. My fascination with this series started in April 2013 and I can say without hesitation that it has been a consistently fabulous series. 'The King' was received with excitement from myself mainly because since book one I've had a soft spot for Wrath, the Alpha warrior King and as a result you can imagine that I've been impatientl</span>
  <span id="freeText9792131685720515666" style="display:none"><b>FIVE ALL HAIL THE KING STARS.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396596046i/9157790._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396596046i/9157791._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>JR Ward has not failed me yet, this series is nothing short of phenomenal and I don't ever want to stop reading about this band of brothers. My fascination with this series started in April 2013 and I can say without hesitation that it has been a consistently fabulous series. 'The King' was received with excitement from myself mainly because since book one I've had a soft spot for Wrath, the Alpha warrior King and as a result you can imagine that I've been impatiently waiting to get my hands all over this novel. There are no words that I can put together to describe how insanely good this series is but for now here are my 'All hail the king' thoughts ...<br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>The throne is at threat from enemies made in secret places and a vigilante group of rebelling vampires that desire to see a change in power. Desperate to keep honour to his families name, Wrath must fight for a throne that was never in his heart to keep. With years of having his beloved, Beth by his side Wrath believes they can overcome almost anything but with change comes unrest and this couple are not only fighting an external battle but they encounter battles from within. Follow the continuing storyline of JR Wards most beloved series where we are also discovering more about surrounding characters, impossible romance and an alpha vampire world that you'll never want to forget.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396596046i/9157792._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396596046i/9157793._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>JR Ward has an imagination that is second to none, her writing style and well thought out story telling is other worldly - quite literally. The Black dagger brotherhood is a series that makes me cry, laugh and smile and there's certainly no escape from 'feeling the heat' Mrs Ward knows how to make her characters burst with lust and longing and she doesn't let her readers fell left out either, her ovary exploding sex scenes would turn a nun to sin. The pages are crammed full with clever twists and turns and ongoing character and story development and I am always kept right on my toes wondering what this author will deliver next. As for 'The King' well I can assuredly confirm that nothing could tear me away from the pages of this novel and as my most anticipated book of 2014 I savoured every single one of the 592 pages. In this particular book of the series you can expect more romance, more action, and more 'getting to know' some additional characters, here JR Ward focuses on the king and queen, Wrath and Beth, Assail the drug lord and his obsession with Sola the human con artist and finally iAm and Trez the mysterious Shadows. Each developing storyline really draws me in, so much so that I have blurred lines of reality when I'm spending time with a JR book. Without question there are not words I have adequate enough to sum up how I feel about this series, JR Ward has me wrapped around her little finger and now I have to wait patiently, or not so patiently in my case for book number thirteen to be revealed. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396649655i/9166180._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396596046i/9157795._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>If it's a gritty, paranormal romance series that you are waiting to sink your teeth into, then you don't want to miss out on the brotherhood. I can't explain how addictive or how obsessive I feel about this series, but I do know that I want everyone to pick up this series and love it as much as I do. I loved the idea that JR Ward has gone full circle with a story about The king and I can only say that this book made me feel a whole range of emotions from loved up to turned on, to heart break to smiling like a mad woman, so much so that I'm sure I'll not forget. If you already love this series then this book will be the icing on the cake and if you've yet to meet the brothers well all I can say is that you are in for a treat. Go grab it readers, release day was April 1st. Enjoy, kisses.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396596738i/9157819._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>**Thanks to my BDB girls for another fang-tastic buddy read. I Love that we do this together, you feel me?**</i>
</b></span>

  <span id="freeText5560683220624130341" style="display:none"><b>4 Long Live the King Stars<br><br><i>To survive one must not be alone.<br>And one must have a partner of worth.<br>Possess that? And you are richer than any King or queen who e'er roamed the earth.</i></b><br><br><i>The players we know...</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397025212i/9220624._SX540_.png" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>But the game is more painful than we could ever imagine...</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397025213i/9220625.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What happens after the HEA? When everyday troubles creep around the corner, family and duties busts your bubble of happiness.<br><br>For a normal couple? Counseling.<br>For the Blind King and his Half-Breed Queen? Hoping to stay together, alive and save the whole race in the meantime.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/20248.J_R__Ward" title="J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">J.R. Ward</a> , delivers the 12th novel in her amazing and intricate Black Dagger Brotherhood with a twist. Rev-visiting the very first and most beloved couple, fighting for the right to stay together and have a chance at happiness.<br><br>As usual, she just can't stay there... At least 5 other characters and their stories complete this story that follows different directions and tries to make us like heroes and villains, virgins and sluts, commoners and glymera aristocrats. <br><br><b>What I liked:</b><br><br>✓ Wrath and Beth.<br>The reigning couple simply RULES!!! It was a huge plus that we were already familiar with their story and we have got glimpses of their struggles throughout the series. Keeping the main focus on them again flowed effortlessly. They stayed true to themselves and they grew. It was also refreshing that the spotlight wasn't on their sexual encounters but their emotional turmoil and helping the whole vampire race for a change. The threat to the throne brought them more close than ever and the ending simply stunned me!<br><br>✓ iAm<br>In a sea of POVs and various characters interrupting my love affair with Wrath, the Shadow was a refreshing new voice. Caustic, ironic, loyal and just unable to not care, the chef is a sight to behold and the only thread in this tangled web of stories that I am excited to read.<br><br>✓ Doc Jane<br>*shameful admition* I wasn't a fan... *ducks head*<br>But book by book, her integrity, loyalty, fierceness and dry wit, won me over. Vishous couldn't have found a better mate, Ghost or not.<br><br>✓ Wrath and Anya<br>Giving us a rare glimpse at the past, we got introduced to Wrath's parents! HOOOOORAY! It was a great emotional sidestory and one of the best parts of the book.<br><br>✓ John Matthews<br>I LOVE HIM. End.<br><br><b>What it bored me:</b><br><br>✗ X'cor and his Bastards<br>Seriously Layla????? Seriously???<br><br>✗ Trez<br>Manslut. End.<br><br>✗ Assail<br>Waste of pages..... Sorry, I couldn't connect at any point. Almost forced to skip...<br><br>✗ Glymera<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397130348ra/9235176.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall assessment: ✓ ♥<br><br>Would it be greedy of me to ask for more Wrath? Well, maybe yeah.... But how about Zhadist? Sounds fair right? I need more <b>Zhadist</b>!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397130348ra/9235177.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>LOL!<br><br><br><i>Pre-release excitement</i><br><i>The next BDB book will take us back, to our first and favourite couple... <br><br><blockquote><b>Wrath son of Wrath and Beth Randall</b></blockquote></i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380315268i/688973.png" width="400" height="310" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>HELL YEEEEEEEEEEEAAAAAAAAAHHH!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380315268ra/688974.gif" width="300" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And................<b>A BABY</b>?!?!?!?!?!!?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/437269.gif" width="324" height="183" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My mind exploded but somehow, it keeps screaming!!!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380315268ra/688975.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Expected publication: March 25th 2014</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/364823.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_576411559" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/576411559" />
    <a title="Midgetbee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8783181-midgetbee"><img alt="Midgetbee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345989286p2/8783181.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/576411559?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Midgetbee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Midgetbee" href="/user/show/8783181-midgetbee">Midgetbee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8783181-midgetbee?shelf=x-2014">x-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8783181-midgetbee?shelf=a-ipad">a-ipad</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8783181-midgetbee?shelf=mine">mine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer576411559" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16074214955419013925">If this was fanfiction it'd be good. But as an entry in the series by the actual author, it's bad. Very bad.<br/><br/>The series started off with the typical PNR conventions of insta-love, but ever since Lover Unbound was let down by a number of fans declaring an undying loathing for its heroine, Ward has branched out into a new form of story-telling. Whereas the first four concentrated solely on the main couple and their story, with a few fights in the war and a hint of subsequent couplings, the books af</span>
  <span id="freeText16074214955419013925" style="display:none">If this was fanfiction it'd be good. But as an entry in the series by the actual author, it's bad. Very bad.<br /><br />The series started off with the typical PNR conventions of insta-love, but ever since Lover Unbound was let down by a number of fans declaring an undying loathing for its heroine, Ward has branched out into a new form of story-telling. Whereas the first four concentrated solely on the main couple and their story, with a few fights in the war and a hint of subsequent couplings, the books after that began to assume a different shape. Subplot after subplot began to emerge, one of which gave us Qhuay, the others finally coalescing in the over-arcing plot in which the glymera (nobility) of the vampire race, dissatisfied with the virtual non-reign of King Wrath, seek his overthrow. <br /><br />Add to this a seeming compulsion of Ward's to introduce at least two new characters and half a dozen subplots into every novel since Lover Unleashed and you discover a real problem; Ward barely has the literary stamina to continue the main plot to its conclusion, let alone six, and she is very easily distracted. Very easily.<br /><br />As a consequence The King suffers. What could easily have been a plot in which the Queen wants a child and tries to convince her hellren of the merits of such an idea during a time of political upheaval, because of Ward's need to throw herself into three different POVs and showcase a different subplot every chapter, instead we get a sequence of events in which both act--quite frankly--like assholes, storming in and out of rooms screaming at each other and throwing tantrums like children. That events such as these tie into the central premise of the book, the attempt to overthrow Wrath, is disconcerting at best. Both characters are now so unattractive personality wise that it is hard to root for the survival of the race, let alone whether or not they get the baby Beth so desperately thinks will solve all her problems.<br /><br />At this point in the series there is a definite feel that Ward is taking things somewhere that the characters themselves don't particularly want to go and the books are so formulaic at this stage it's easy to call events before you see them. As a result whereas once an idle daydream of spending an evening in the mansion may have been a pleasant way to pass the time, in order to make the revisits and subplots happen everyone has been made so damned stupid and unpleasant that making your way through a new Brotherhood novel is more of an achievement then entertainment and the pushing forward of her favourites, Assail and Doc Jane in particular, only compounds this.<br /><br />Assail is an obvious retelling of a still existent character with every single redeeming quality removed in an attempt to make him edgy and while Doc Jane is one of the Brotherhood's two doctors and as such should be featured, the prevalence of medical emergencies in every novel since her introduction in Lover Unbound and the attempt at reworking her relationship with Vishous in Lover Unleashed mean that things have gotten to the point where it's a wonder someone can open a door without shattering their arm, leading to a visit in the clinic with the Spectral Surgeon if only so the hurt character can go into raptures about how lovely and awesome she is. As a result no less then two characters completely unrelated to the Brothers have recently been allowed in the apparently super secret compound the Brothers live in, just so they can be treated by Ward's favourite female.<br /><br />While this may seem completely innocuous by itself (and reveal my detestation of that character), it highlights Ward's willingness to throw out the rules of her own world-building in order to push forward certain characters or resolve problems with an easy and completely nonsensical solution, which has been achieved so far by making her characters completely and unerringly stupid. Unfortunately such an approach demands that her readers dumb themselves down too, or at least develop the memory capabilities of a goldfish, as she often seeks to rationalise unpopular actions in subsequent novels. An example of this being the new rules about bonding. In the books prior to Lover Reborn we were told that bonding is a permanent attachment and that if a female died, her bonded mate would be so devastated that he he couldn't live without her, an action that rationalised the need to find a way for Mary and Doc Jane's continued presences in the novels and find a way for their HEA.<br /><br />Unfortunately the events of Lover Reborn and Ward's need to push these events as commonplace completely undermine the central drama of The King. If Tohr, a bonded male, can move on from his shellan's death and find love and happiness with another as a number of others are described as doing in this book, then why can't Wrath? Sure, Beth dying from pregnancy would be bad for him for a while, but with the idea of bonding shorn of all association with the concept of forever, it's hard to think that Wrath wouldn't find someone else he likes just as much a few books later. Coupled with the realisation that with the exception of Wellsie every female has found a way to come back even if the worst has happened, the tension disappears completely.<br /><br />This could've been countered with a compelling installment of the plot to overthrow Wrath, now including newish characters the Band of Bastards, and while the book does contain a degree of uncertainty on that issue for most of its span, the ending is so completely, utterly, and unfailingly stupid that I felt insulted as a reader. It couldn't be more obvious that Ward couldn't plot a political storyline if her life depended on it and as such we are expected to deal with a few scenes of utter bullshit at the end that if thought about for more then a moment, actually creates more problems for their society then it solves. But Ward wanted it wrapped up in order to concentrate on other things. With a seeming conclusion of the Wrath and Beth storyline on a personal front, the political had to be finished up too. It's just a shame there was less time dedicated to an apparent major societal shift then there was to Sola's time thinking how about kind Doc Jane was. Even if it did leave everything exactly the same.<br /><br />And therein lies the problem. Whereas the first four books concentrated in the personal, when something outside of the couple happened, you had the feeling it mattered and that things had changed. Now, no matter what happens everything always ends the same. There may be a new couple or a new baby, but the same people are in the same places--unless they've moved into the mansion-- and everyone's a little less appealing as a result.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16074214955419013925" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1968869011" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8210101289781313880"><b>5 “Long live the King.” Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/edYpA_zpsxerbgw8x.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492127575ra/22485536.gif' alt=' photo edYpA_zpsxerbgw8x.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b> Spoilers</b><br/><br/>First read 2014<br/>Reread 4/13/2017<br/><br/><b>“I’m goin’ nowhere, leelan. You don’t worry about a goddamn thing. Understand me?” Beth wanted to believe him. Needed to. But she feared it was a promise far harder to keep than speak. “Beth?” “Make love to me.” It was the only truth she could put out there that wouldn’t burst the bubble. “Please.” He kissed her once. Twice. And then started to move again. “Always, leelan. Always.”-Wrath and Beth</b><br/><br/>I loved The King! It was so </span>
  <span id="freeText8210101289781313880" style="display:none"><b>5 “Long live the King.” Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/edYpA_zpsxerbgw8x.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492127575ra/22485536.gif" alt=" photo edYpA_zpsxerbgw8x.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> Spoilers</b><br><br>First read 2014<br>Reread 4/13/2017<br><br><b>“I’m goin’ nowhere, leelan. You don’t worry about a goddamn thing. Understand me?” Beth wanted to believe him. Needed to. But she feared it was a promise far harder to keep than speak. “Beth?” “Make love to me.” It was the only truth she could put out there that wouldn’t burst the bubble. “Please.” He kissed her once. Twice. And then started to move again. “Always, leelan. Always.”-Wrath and Beth</b><br><br>I loved The King! It was so good. I love when long running series retouch past favorite couples. The King of course is about Wrath and Beth with little bits of the whole gang sprinkled in. And as with all Black Dagger Brotherhood books there are other story plots going on in this book as well. We have Assail and Sola, Xcor and Layla, Trez and Selena, and a surprising plot line of Wrath's father and mother Wrath(Sr) and Anha. Can I just say that Wrath's parents were so sweet and damn was Wrath Sr sexy. I totally see where the son gets it. I loved getting to see Wrath Sr fall so hard for Anha and make her his one and only. It was a little bitter sweet though since anyone following the series knows that Wrath Sr. and Anha are horrifically murdered in front of their pretran son. I still loved getting to know them and see the parallels between the father and son. I knew when I finished the last book that Wrath and Beth were going to be having some problems since Beth caught baby fever and Wrath didn't want a child. <br><br><b>“I need you to hear this,” he said in a dead voice, “and know that it’s the God’s honest. I will not service you in your needing. Ever.” Now it was her turn to breathe out like she’d been socked in the gut. “I can’t … I can’t believe you just said that.” “It is never, ever going to happen. I will never get you pregnant.”-Wrath and Beth</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/111915-just-give-me-your-sperm-gif-jl-DBrq_zps5ycak3yv.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492127575ra/22485538.gif" alt=" photo 111915-just-give-me-your-sperm-gif-jl-DBrq_zps5ycak3yv.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“You can call me Pastor—and before Mr. Sox Fan gets his panties in a wad, I want everyone to know I’m legit. I went online, took a minister’s course in under an hour, and I’m ordained, baby.” Rhage raised his hand. “Pastor Ass-hat, I have a question.” “Yes, my son, you are going to hell.”-Lassiter and Rhage</b><br><br>Even though I hated seeing Beth and Wrath fight, I loved seeing them grow in their relationship. All couples have ups and downs and I felt J.R. Ward keeps that real in this series. I totally got were both Wrath and Beth were coming from. I loved that even though Wrath was scared to get Beth pregnant he decided to go for it anyways. Although she was already 4 months pregnant and they just didn't know it. And OMG the way Wrath acted when he found out they were having a son was so damn cute I was smiling like a crazy woman. Now having a child wasn't the only problem Wrath and Beth were having in this book. Xcor was at it again getting the glymera to declare that Wrath can't be King because he mated a half breed and their heir wouldn't be full blooded vampire. I hated Beth's guilt over something she couldn't help, and I hated the glymera more than ever for them using his love to try and strip Wrath of his throne. I loved that Beth was the one that came up with the solution. Vampire mate divorce and a human wedding. The human wedding which was done by Lassiter was hilarious but very sweet too. I also loved Wrath embraced his blindness in this book. He accepted himself and really grew as a mate, father, and King. <br><br><b>“…a son?” “Yes. A son.” All of a sudden, he felt the biggest, widest, happiest grin hit his face, the goddamn thing stretching his cheeks until they hurt, making his eyes water from the strain, pulling at his temples until they burned. And the joy wasn’t just on his puss. A flush so great it burned him alive flooded through his body, cleansing him in places he didn’t know were dirty, washing out cobwebs that had crept into his corners, making him feel alive in a way he hadn’t been in a very, very long time. Before he knew what he was doing, he burst to his feet with Beth in his arms, leaned back, and hollered at the top of his lungs, with more pride than his six-foot-nine frame could hold. “A soooooooooooooooooooooooooooooooooooooon! I’m having a soooooooooooooooooooooooon!”-Wrath and Beth</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/Bethwrathandlittlewrath_zpsq03cka7d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492127575i/22485537._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Bethwrathandlittlewrath_zpsq03cka7d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“My brother.” Z shoved out his palm, his scarred face in a half smile, his yellow eyes warm. “Congratulations.” Instead of shaking anything, Wrath shoved that ultrasound picture into his Brother’s face. “Do you see him? See my son? He’s big, right, Beth?” She kissed Nalla’s super soft hair. “Yes.” “Big and healthy, right?” Beth laughed some more. “Big and healthy. Absolutely perfect.” “Perfect!” Wrath bellowed. “And this is a doctor saying it—I mean, she went to medical school.” Even Z started laughing at that point. Beth gave Nalla back to her parents. “And Dr. Sam told me she’s delivered over fifteen thousand babies over the course of her career—” “See!” Wrath yelled. “She knows these things. My son is perfect! Where’s the champagne? Fritz! Get the fucking champagne!”-Z, Wrath, and Beth</b><br><br>Normally I am bored with the Assail and Sola plot but I really enjoyed it in this book. I loved seeing Assail save Sola. I melted a little when he bonded with her. Their relationship really started in this book for me. Their passion was strong in this book. I liked Assail a lot more in this book. At times though there are things about him I really dislike. Like his drug use. Their relationship was rocky and ended with a to be continued feel, but the connection was there and strong. I am looking forward to seeing where these two go. I really don't care about Trez and the forced mating plot. I am however a little intrigued by the Selena and Trez story line. I think they are cute together. What the hell is up with Selena's illness? I liked that iAm was more talkative in this book. He seemed very sweet and I think it was cute that he has never been with a woman before. I have always loved John Matthew and I was so glad he was in this book a lot. It was so sweet seeing him and Beth in a close relationship. I loved how supportive Xhex was of John's seizures. I really wish everyone including John knew John was Darius. Not that it really takes away anything that they don't but I just wish they knew. Abalone and his daughter were new characters in this book. It was fun to see Abalone's father and Wrath's father's relationship and comparing it to his and Wrath. Now for my favorite side plot Xcor and Layla. God I don't know what it is about that chosen and bastard but I just love them. I eat up ever single minute I can with them. I love how sweet Xcor gets around her. I love how vulnerable he is with her but still puts himself out there because he wants her that much. I love how drawn Layla is to him. How she doesn't see him as ugly but fierce, and worthy. That part with Xcor at the mall buying nice clothes for his kinda date with Layla was funny as fuck. I can't wait to get their story. The King was an amazing and fun read. <br><br><b>“I abolished the monarchy last night.” Cue the crickets. “What …?” she said. "You told me you didn’t want to be the cause of my giving up the throne. You weren’t. In the end, it was my choice. Sooner or later, someone else is going to make a run at me—and by extension you and him. And then if I die? My son’s going to end up having to fight to keep something that shouldn’t be decided by bloodline. It should be decided by merit.” Beth put her hands up to her face. “Oh, my God…” “So we’re a democracy now. Saxton helped make it legal. And elections are going to take place in a little while. I’ve talked to Abalone—he’s going to coordinate it all. Hell, the guy already had a good slate of candidates. Oh, and the best thing? The glymera’s out of a job. I did away with the Council. See ya, motherfuckers.”-Wrath </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8210101289781313880" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/897760869?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Exina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Exina" href="/user/show/5309539-exina">Exina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=married-established-couple">married-established-couple</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer897760869" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1711714200864173283"><i>
  <b>April 5, 2014</b>
</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Sometimes, you didn’t get what you wanted. <br/>But if you had all you needed?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>2.5 stars</b><br/><br/><i>The King</i> is one of the most anticipated books of the year, book 12 of the Black Dagger Brotherhood series. <br/><br/>Book 11, <i>Lover at Last</i> was a huge disappointment, so I had no intention of reading further books of the series, but I’ve read it anyway. <br/><br/>Why? <br/><br/>Well, I realized this series is more and more like... no, actually <b>it IS a soap opera.</b> You don’t really want to watch, or read it anymore, b</span>
  <span id="freeText1711714200864173283" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>April 5, 2014</b>
</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Sometimes, you didn’t get what you wanted. <br>But if you had all you needed?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>2.5 stars</b><br><br><i>The King</i> is one of the most anticipated books of the year, book 12 of the Black Dagger Brotherhood series. <br><br>Book 11, <i>Lover at Last</i> was a huge disappointment, so I had no intention of reading further books of the series, but I’ve read it anyway. <br><br>Why? <br><br>Well, I realized this series is more and more like... no, actually <b>it IS a soap opera.</b> You don’t really want to watch, or read it anymore, but you want to know what happens to the characters because you care for them, and somehow, throughout the years, they grew to your heart.<br><br>But it couldn’t live up even to my already low expectations…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396549284ra/9150381.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Sadly, many! </b><br><br><b>Wrath and Beth.</b> Their storyline is obvious and very predictable: they fight about having a child or not, but have it anyway, ending with a forced giving-birth drama, but everything is going to be okay. After all, it’s a romance, not a tragedy. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396703580i/9174423._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Wrath</b> is magnificent and imposing, as always. He is a born ruler, just not always aware of that. I loved the way Ward portrayed the change in him, not only about having a child, but about his approach to the death of his parents, and to the throne as well. <br><blockquote>He thought back to the night his parents had been slaughtered. The one thing they had done before that door had been broken down? Hide him. Keep him safe. Preserve him—and it hadn’t been about ensuring the future of the throne. That was not at all what they’d said as they’d locked him in that crawl space.<br><i>I love you.</i><br>That had been the only message that had mattered when their time had run out. Not, <i>Be a good King.</i> Not, <i>Follow in my footsteps.</i> Not, <i>Make me proud or else …</i><br><i>I love you.</i><br>It was the tie that bound, even across the divides of death and time.</blockquote><br>Not everything is perfect in this storyline, especially the end, but his feelings, fears, frustrations, self-poisonous thoughts are nicely presented. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396703580i/9174424._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <i>He realized he, too, was finally free — and that his parents, if they had had a chance to look over his shoulder, would have approved of him.<br>Just the way he was.</i>
</blockquote><br>I was bored to death by <b>Beth</b>’s continuous, repetitive, and often hysterical musings on every little detail of her thoughts and everyday actions, even when she had to go to pee. She is such an irritating character here! How I despise her selfishness and immature behavior! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396703580ra/9174425.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are many <b>secondary storylines,</b> and first it seems there is much going on in this book, but actually not much happens. It can be easily summarized on a couple of pages. The plot is fragmented, tiring, and unnecessarily elongated.<br><br><b>Things I couldn’t find in this book: </b><br> - originality, <br> - action and thrill, <br> - twists and turns, <br> - surprises, <br> - <i>lessers,</i> or any capable foe, <br> - real drama, <br> - steamy erotic scenes (because they are lukewarm and/or frustrating).<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396703759ra/9174473.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Things in large quantities: </b><br> - secondary storylines and viewpoints, <br> - unnecessary scenes (for example who cares about how Xcor is peeling an apple or about the luxury of the foyer for the millionth time?), <br> - musings, inner monologues, emotional rantings, <br> - exhausting and irritating pop-culture references, <br> - overlong descriptions about nothing, <br> - boring recollections, and repetitive thoughts. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386001ra/745204.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Things almost made me punch something, or someone:</b><br> - Beth<br> - iAm and Trez are the slightly modified equivalents of Phury and Zsadist. So unimaginative. <br> - Beth’s almost Twilight-type pregnancy. Ward misled me for a couple of chapters, and the explanation was not satisfying. <br> - Writing style as a whole: pop-culture references, slang, acronyms, abbreviations, mutilated words (abso, obvi).<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396703580ra/9174427.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Of course, there are scenes I enjoyed:</b><br> - many scenes of Wrath’s (as I mentioned above)<br> - Assail’s quest for Sola <br> - Sola gets free from her captors<br> - the wedding ceremony performed by Lassiter (this scene lacks originality too, but at least it is hilarious)<br> - S’Ex’s scenes<br><blockquote>
  <i>“Let me make myself perfectly clear. You touch iAm and I will find you. Your last breath will be mine and your heart will still be warm when I take it out of your chest and eat it raw.”<br>“You know, it’s a wonder we don’t get along better.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>All in all</b><br><br>I didn’t expected much, so I’m not disappointed, but sadly I’m not pleasantly surprised either. <br><br>Oh, almost forgot how unsatisfied I was with the baby’s name. I hoped they would name him <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Darius, but Beth named him Wrath, and started to refer to her husband as Big Wrath, and to her son as Little Wrath, later LW. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <b> Arrrgh!!!</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="1711714200864173283" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_643273695" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/643273695" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/643273695?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer643273695" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18136471990516189928"><b>5 Blind King stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/604d25c2-3648-4c8a-b417-80d7a846f473_zpsb9f110d8.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396790534i/9187329.jpg' alt=' photo 604d25c2-3648-4c8a-b417-80d7a846f473_zpsb9f110d8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I’ve been waiting all year for this book. The 12th book in the Black Dagger Brotherhood. I am obsessed with this series, can’t get enough of my boys. This author could write dozens more books and I would keep on reading. I loved the idea of going back to the beginning- to an original brother. I may have been a little concerned since we’ve already had a Wrath book, but I shouldn’t have been. It was fantastic! <br/><br/>I find these books incredibly difficult to review. In each book, </span>
  <span id="freeText18136471990516189928" style="display:none"><b>5 Blind King stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/604d25c2-3648-4c8a-b417-80d7a846f473_zpsb9f110d8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396790534i/9187329.jpg" alt=" photo 604d25c2-3648-4c8a-b417-80d7a846f473_zpsb9f110d8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’ve been waiting all year for this book. The 12th book in the Black Dagger Brotherhood. I am obsessed with this series, can’t get enough of my boys. This author could write dozens more books and I would keep on reading. I loved the idea of going back to the beginning- to an original brother. I may have been a little concerned since we’ve already had a Wrath book, but I shouldn’t have been. It was fantastic! <br><br>I find these books incredibly difficult to review. In each book, we have the main couple’s story (Wrath and Beth in this particular book) but that’s only the half of it. The other half follows several other characters. I will try to quickly review each smaller story along with the Blind King’s and his half-breed Queens.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/86b8e56c-88e6-4afa-9557-7a4f7cf9489e_zps68e6be70.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396790534i/9187330.jpg" alt=" photo 86b8e56c-88e6-4afa-9557-7a4f7cf9489e_zps68e6be70.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“You know what? That shit’s not worth it to me. You’re what’s important. You’re what matters. Everything else- everyone else can fuck off.”</blockquote>
</i><br> <b>Wrath and Beth</b><br>Wrath and Beth have a lot going on. Wrath is getting threatened by many to take what is rightfully his. The throne. Although he never wanted it, it’s his father’s Legacy and he doesn’t want it stolen from him. Wrath loves his Shellan more than anything, the throne included. Beth and Wrath don’t have the easiest journey. I won’t go into the big storyline, but there are issues between them. <br><br>I’ve always liked Beth and Wrath, but compared to some of the other brother’s stories, their tale in Dark Lover didn’t stack up. I am glad to say that I loved THIS chapter of their story more than the first. I fell more in love with the King!<br><i>
  <blockquote>“I want you to know something,” he said into her hair. As she went still, he tried to pull something worth hearing out of his ass. Some string of words that were even in the same zip code as what was doing in his chest.<br><br>“What?” she whispered.<br><br>“You are everything to me.”<br><br>It was so incredibly, totally not enough- and yet she sighed and melted into him like that was all she wanted to hear. And a bag of chips. <br><br>Sometimes you got lucky.</blockquote>
</i><br><b>Xcor and Layla</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/9f91cc67-16bf-45ff-83aa-ee635594a5f4_zps3b0e6cb8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396790534i/9187331.jpg" alt=" photo 9f91cc67-16bf-45ff-83aa-ee635594a5f4_zps3b0e6cb8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Speaking of the throne being threatened... Xcor is one of the ringleaders. He is the leader of the Band of Bastards. And in his quest to take down the King, he has fallen for the unattainable. The Chosen, Layla. The Chosen that is pregnant by Qhuinn. Layla has unexplainable feelings for Xcor. She knows he isn’t ‘good’, but is he as bad as he seems? I feel Xcor is on the path of redemption.<br><i>
  <blockquote>In this moment of triumph, the only place he wanted to be was with the female he could not have.</blockquote>
</i> And one of the funnies scenes in the book was his shopping trip...<br><i>
  <blockquote>“Knock her dead, my man.” <br>“Oh, no.” Xcor shook his head. “That shan’t be necessary. This one I like.”</blockquote>
</i> I am very much looking forward to more of these two in the future, hopefully they will get their own book soon! <br><br><b>Trez and Selena</b>  <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/89f7b1aa-1d8e-44b3-a8d8-27a42a1aa230_zps3b399753.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396790534i/9187332.jpg" alt=" photo 89f7b1aa-1d8e-44b3-a8d8-27a42a1aa230_zps3b399753.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>We’ve gotten to know the Shadows pretty well since Rehv’s book. I love them both equally in different ways. The King focus’s a lot on Trez’s story. Trez is trying to get away from his future. The future he was sold into, the one he doesn’t want. iAm will do anything in his power to help, but things aren’t looking good. The Chosen Selena has feelings for Trez. He feels them too, but he also feels unworthy of her. Their story was left wide open, I’m anxious to see where it goes. <br><br><b>Assail and Sola</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/e2c7909c-2e59-40b2-ab15-27f26ea26ebb_zpsfc9addfb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396790534i/9187333.jpg" alt=" photo e2c7909c-2e59-40b2-ab15-27f26ea26ebb_zpsfc9addfb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>  I’m not gonna lie... Assail was a crazy motherfucker. And I adored him! He is also one of those characters that isn’t a ‘good’ guy, but not a bad guy either. He’s stuck in between. Sola, his little burglar has gotten herself into some trouble. Even though it’s not in his nature, Assail feels compelled to help her. He wants her. Their story was also unresolved so we’ll see where it takes us... <br><br><br><br><br>As soon as I finished the book, I was instantly curious about who the next book would be about. There were several possibilities, obviously the three above were most likely. When I found out the 13th book in this series would be called <b>The Shadows</b>, I was stoked. Not only do I want more Trez and Selena, but after that little bomb iAm dropped on us, I can’t wait for his story! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/be2a684c-e2e2-468c-8595-82e0e4164992_zps4c3fad55.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396766888i/9184990.jpg" alt=" photo be2a684c-e2e2-468c-8595-82e0e4164992_zps4c3fad55.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This series is spectacular. Full of romance, suspense, steam, action and twists and turns. I can’t get enough of these books. When I start reading, the characters and stories captivate me. I feel sucked into this world. I have such a strong connection to the characters and their stories. I just can’t get enough! Thankfully, Ms. Ward isn’t planning on ending this series anytime soon- we have at least three more books to look forward to in the Brotherhood series! Bring it on!<br><br><br><b>ALL HAIL THE KING!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="18136471990516189928" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2561643929" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2561643929" />
    <a title="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com"><img alt="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570843185p2/70316517.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2561643929?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" href="/user/show/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com">Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2561643929" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11323410729252344767"><b>In chess, the Queen protects the King.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1573537504i/28437797.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If you like the Black Dagger Brotherhood, you can’t help but like Wrath and feel for him. I mean he is the toughest of all the BDB warriors, he never wanted to be the King, all he really wants to do is fight against their enemies, but the fact that he lost his sight prevents him from going out on patrol with his brothers like he wants. Even though he can fight as good as anyone despite his blindness, he gets stuck in his office doing paperwork. <br/><br/>So many thing</span>
  <span id="freeText11323410729252344767" style="display:none"><b>In chess, the Queen protects the King.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1573537504i/28437797.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you like the Black Dagger Brotherhood, you can’t help but like Wrath and feel for him. I mean he is the toughest of all the BDB warriors, he never wanted to be the King, all he really wants to do is fight against their enemies, but the fact that he lost his sight prevents him from going out on patrol with his brothers like he wants. Even though he can fight as good as anyone despite his blindness, he gets stuck in his office doing paperwork. <br><br>So many things happen in this book, not only between Wrath and Beth, but in other parts of the ongoing storylines. One of the main things that picks up in this book where the last book left off is the fact that the human thief, Sola Morte, was kidnapped at her Gran’s house. If you have read the previous books you will remember that she was hired by Benloise to spy on Assail, the drug dealer. <br><br>Assail is very interested in Sola, especially after Benloise shafted her in the payment he owed her and she retaliated by breaking into Benloise’s house, and moving one of his statues a bit off center, barely moving it, but apparently he is such a perfectionist that she knows something like that will really piss him off. Apparently she didn’t know just how much because, he had her kidnapped and brought to a house where he has people tortured to death.<br><br>Another storyline is the thing that happens to John Matthew when he gets near Beth. He feels some strange connection, then has a sort of seizure. We have seen where John Matthew is sometimes remembering things that only Darius should know. Beth is Darius’ daughter and John Matthew is his son, so they are half-siblings even though they didn’t meet until one of the early books in the series. <br><br>It is looking more and more like either John Matthew is the reincarnation of Darius or has some sort of weird connection to the dead Warrior, in addition to being his son. I have read in the wiki that John is Darius reincarnated, but frankly I think it is something else, like the the soul of Darius is inside John, but so is his own. Though what do I know? That could be the definition of reincarnation.<br> <br>The storyline about the shadows, Trez Latimer and his bother iAm, is also in this book. You really have to feel for these guys. Trez was sold by his parents to the Queen of the S’Hsibe when he was young and is meant to be the stud to the queens daughter. Basically that will entail a life of sexual servitude in a gilded cage. Trez and iAm left their home for that reason, but they keep getting calls from the Queens High Priest for Trez to return. <br><br>Trez will not answer the phone when the High Priest calls, so it falls to iAm to take care of. iAm is constantly taking care of Trez, whether it be when he is downed by one of his frequent migraines or whether he is just trying to get Trez to change his lifestyle. Apparently back home they think of their bodies as temples and even have strict rites when it comes to the sexual act. Starting with bathing and keeping their temple clean. Which is why Trez is so rebellious and he does it with human women so often in just about any way and any place he can. Though now he is starting to really feel something for the chosen, Selena. <br><br>Beth wants a baby, and after seeing Wrath nearly bleed out in a prior book when he was shot by XCor, she wants it even more. She feels that then if something happened to him, at least she would have a part of him. However, Wrath knows that the death rate is high among pregnant female vampires, and he doesn’t want to chance losing Beth. They are at odds with each other on that point and the fact that Wrath is working so hard in a job he hates isn’t making things easier. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1573803486i/28452297.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I really enjoyed this book. I had a long break between the last book and this one because it is a bit hard to read 500-600 page books with the same ongoing storylines one after the other for 10+ books, it is almost like one exceedingly long book. However, the break did me good and I am totally into the lives of the Black Dagger Brotherhood all over again. I really can’t wait to hear what happens to Trez in his book and I am especially waiting to see how (and if) Xcor and Layla get together. <br><br><a href="https://www.ilikebooksbest.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a>|<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/wennel" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a>|<a href="https://www.facebook.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>|<a href="https://smile.amazon.com/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AFFE5A2BGXJQTQMCYHFC4YHV6KFQ?preview=true" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a>|<a href="https://www.twitter.com/wendysu020202" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>|<a href="https://www.bookbub.com/profile/1895823057" rel="nofollow noopener">BookBub</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11323410729252344767" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_576275529" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/576275529" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/576275529?book_show_action=true">Mar 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=angels-nephilim-and-demons">angels-nephilim-and-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=multiple-pov">multiple-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer576275529" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6618796335653965305"><b>I finally finished the book!</b> My first in April, actually. Yes, it's the 14th. It's called real life, bitches. Sometimes books take a backseat. <br/><br/>By now, most of the die-hard fans who were going to read this have already done so. I've seen the complaints. I share a few of the complaints.<br/><br/>But it's Ward. She's like this comfort-food writer for me. Even when it's bad, I always know that I'll laugh a few times, and will get at the very least a few moments of good sexual tension. So I keep reading.<br/><br/><b>But de</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6618796335653965305" style="display:none"><b>I finally finished the book!</b> My first in April, actually. Yes, it's the 14th. It's called real life, bitches. Sometimes books take a backseat. <br /><br />By now, most of the die-hard fans who were going to read this have already done so. I've seen the complaints. I share a few of the complaints.<br /><br />But it's Ward. She's like this comfort-food writer for me. Even when it's bad, I always know that I'll laugh a few times, and will get at the very least a few moments of good sexual tension. So I keep reading.<br /><br /><b>But dear me, even I couldn't ignore the fifty PoV's this time.</b> I was one of the people who didn't mind when the series left the cookie-cutter PNR format in favor of a more broad-scaled world at around book 7. The extra PoV's were helpful in getting me excited for future stories to come. Yes, sometimes the extras overtook the main story, and I wasn't always a fan of that. But I generally liked the side stories as well, with a few exceptions (I've never been a fan of the lengthy flashbacks). <br /><br /><b>However, it's gotten out of hand.</b> Between iAm, Trez, Xcor, Assail, Throe, Saxton, etc. (including the flip side with the female PoV's) <i>and</i> the flashbacks, <i>plus</i> the current Wrath/Beth story...yeah. We were more than maxed out on PoV's. <br /><br /><b>That said...</b> It was really only the Assail/Sola story which didn't work for me. A lot of people like this couple, but I've never attached to them. I'm still in the Xcor/Layla camp. And I was surprised by how much I enjoyed Trez/Selena's chemistry in this book. I love how Trez isn't the traditional white male character. And since Xcor isn't attractive at all (not like how Z is scarred but you can tell he's still hot), I love that too. Ward's starting to write a little out of her comfort zone. <br /><br /><b>And iam?!?</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Virgin! Yay! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Yay! Yay! Yay!<br /><br />I know that so many people are throwing in the towel. I won't be. The familiarity and brotherhood and awesome sexual chemistry keeps me coming back, even when it takes me WEEKS to read the darn book because of parts that drag. <br /><br />The pros are still outweighing the cons. Maybe it won't always be this way, but sometimes I need to have something familiar to fall back on when I'm tired of constantly having to start new books and learn new characters. Familiar works for me in this instance. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6618796335653965305" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10841494007668178894"><b>3,5 stars</b><br/>Do I like The Black Dagger Brotherhood Series???? No, I MORE THAN LIKE IT………………<br/><blockquote>
