I lost my all-time favorite boyfriend…<img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417119313i/12226870.jpg' alt=' photo 58149773fb8f3eee55d2c5550a8a61df_zps0d57f9b6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>…yes, Qhuinn left me for someone else!!!!!<br/>Anyway, I have moved on…..and what better way than…..yay….more about Wrath & Beth….i adore the King & Queen of all Vampires….<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417119313i/12226871.jpg' alt=' photo BannerBooksBlackDaggerBrotherhoo-26_zps68eb84cd.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So, I get THE KING the day it comes out…I am so excited, over the moon…..<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417119313i/12226872._SY540_.png' alt=' photo 351af7d0-a0c4-4e29-8e49-2d00896c1134_zpsf5de6702.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And by page 116….I give up…impossi</span>
  <span id="freeText10841494007668178894" style="display:none"><b>3,5 stars</b><br>Do I like The Black Dagger Brotherhood Series???? No, I MORE THAN LIKE IT………………<br><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417119854i/12227663.jpg" alt=" photo Black_Dagger_Brotherhood_by_AidanG_zps4b42bafe.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><br>I have a secret to tell..….I was absolutely shattered after Lover at Last…..<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417119313ra/12226869.gif" alt=" photo wnoy5_zps6vkuydj5.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>…yes I did. I lost my all-time favorite boyfriend…<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417119313i/12226870.jpg" alt=" photo 58149773fb8f3eee55d2c5550a8a61df_zps0d57f9b6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>…yes, Qhuinn left me for someone else!!!!!<br>Anyway, I have moved on…..and what better way than…..yay….more about Wrath &amp; Beth….i adore the King &amp; Queen of all Vampires….<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417119313i/12226871.jpg" alt=" photo BannerBooksBlackDaggerBrotherhoo-26_zps68eb84cd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, I get THE KING the day it comes out…I am so excited, over the moon…..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417119313i/12226872._SY540_.png" alt=" photo 351af7d0-a0c4-4e29-8e49-2d00896c1134_zpsf5de6702.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And by page 116….I give up…impossible!!!! How can this be??? This is my all time favorite series….I cannot continue…………..and for months I have avoided opening up page 117…….talk about confused!!!!<br><br>No, I have to go back …..I can’t give up…not now!!!!<br><br>Okay, page 117, 118….next page and well, it was kind of surprising but I actually finished THE KING!!!!<br><br>Did I love it???? Oooh, so sad…but wait, I did like it…just not my favorite …a real pity!!! Now, what was it exactly that it did not “snap and crackle” for me????<br><br>Was this not Wrath &amp; Beth’s book??? That’s what I thought..instead there is not much happening here with these two………because we have all these other characters and couples that, IMHO just got in the way…..like..<br><br>Assail &amp; Marisol…I get it…their story has to be set up for their future book..but did I have to get so much about them…allright, I like Marisol (hell, I hate the shortened version of Sola…her full name is gorgeous…), she’s a kickass exotic…a Brazilian thief….heroine with the most lovable grandmother….but then she’s in lust for Assail, who I HAVE NOT engaged with…never mind that he’s sexy, gorgeous and is nice to her grandmother and his family…he’s still a mobster and drug dealer…….it’s going to take a lot for him to redeem himself to me!!!<br><br>Then Trez, the Shadow and his HUGE LUST for the lovely and virginal Chosen, named Selena!!! Let me just say that he and his brother IAm have not done it for me in the previous books. Still uncertain about Trez…all that “pussy-footing” around Selena just got on my nerves so many times. However, I actually began to like I’AM…..in fact I found it totally endearing….how could I not if Boo (remember Beth’s cat!!) loves him!!!! Now, having been given the news that the next novel will be on the Shadow Brothers….not sure if I am that excited about it!!!!<br><br>Where are all the BDB brothers and their shellans??? A snip here and there…Xhex and JM….a few pages…a page or two with Tohrment…no Autumn…then a teaser with Zsadist and Bella……and nothing, okay a page or two with Qhuinn!!!!! Heartbroken!!!! Me, it was!!!!<br><br>And no action whatsoever….no Lessers, just the boring glymera characters!!!! Where are the fighting brothers????? I wanted more of my BDB heroes...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417119854i/12227664._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_static_tumblr_static__1280_zps7622a3bf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was so pro-Layla before but this whole “work-up” romance with Xcor was a total disaster for me!!!!! I felt no connection between their one or two secret hook-ups….no, relax, the two haven’t done the deed yet!!!!! I still want her to be with someone else….I AM NOT A XCOR fan!!!!!<br><br>What redeemed this book from being..uhm….not a total loss was LW….LITTLE WRATH!!!! <br><blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417119313i/12226873.jpg" alt=" photo 7c11824fe77b40af152eaaff37dcaad6_zps5d30987c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>I am beyond in love with this BDB Prince!!!! I want more of him in the future!!!! See, that’s why I am going to get the next book…..because of LW!!!!<br><br><blockquote><b>“A soooooooooooooooooooooon! I'm having a sooooooooooooooooooooooooon!” </b></blockquote><br><br>One of my favourite parts in this book was when Lassiter “played” the pastor at Wrath &amp; Beth’s “human” marriage ceremony………<br><blockquote><b>“Okay, so, Beth, follow me. 'I, Beth, a totally awesome chick ...'"<br><br>Beth barked out a giggle. "I, Beth ..."<br><br>"Where's the 'awesome chick' part? What? Come on, I have a license from the Internet. I know what I'm doing."<br><br>Wrath nodded at his leehan. "He's right. You are, in fact, awesome. I think we need to hear it."<br><br>"Can I get an amen!" Lassiter shouted.<br><br>"Ammmmmmmmmen!" echoed throughout the mansion.<br><br>"Fine, fine, fine," she said. "I, Beth, a totally awesome chick ..."<br><br>"'... take this meathead, Wrath ...'"<br><br>"... take this meathead, Wrath ..."<br><br>"'... as my husband to have and to hold from this day forward...”</b></blockquote><br>Lassiter….I so want his book….he’s so fabulous!!!!<br><blockquote><b>“By the power vested in me thanks to Google, I know pronounce you husband and wife! You may kiss the bride!” </b></blockquote><br><br>To end my long “tirade”, let’s just say…..not the best in the series but certainly not going to end my affair with BDB!!!!!!</span>

<div id="review_678577896" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/678577896" />
    <a title="Erica Ravenclaw" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12099580-erica-ravenclaw"><img alt="Erica Ravenclaw" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598276462p2/12099580.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/678577896?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erica Ravenclaw" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erica Ravenclaw" href="/user/show/12099580-erica-ravenclaw">Erica Ravenclaw</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer678577896" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6287572862149292220">☆ ☆ <br/><br/><b> No spoilers and and definitely colorful language abound! </b><br/><br/><pre> <b> Oh, how the mighty have fallen. </b> </pre><br/><br/>Sigh.<br/><br/>The King is upon us, and as a loyal, albeit disgruntled fan, I proceeded with caution. Despite the arduous and at times hysterical journey, I have triumphed. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/Halloween%20Upload/GIFS/tumblr_inline_mnijcpINDA1qz4rgp_zps01e3a981.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396902888ra/9201014.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_inline_mnijcpINDA1qz4rgp_zps01e3a981.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>It was exactly 3% that I realized the error of my ways. I like many of you awaited the publication of what I hoped to be Wards return to her former glory, reconnecting with the characters who started it all. With an omnipresent sense of</span>
  <span id="freeText6287572862149292220" style="display:none">☆ ☆ <br><br><b> No spoilers and and definitely colorful language abound! </b><br><br><pre> <b> Oh, how the mighty have fallen. </b> </pre><br><br>Sigh.<br><br>The King is upon us, and as a loyal, albeit disgruntled fan, I proceeded with caution. Despite the arduous and at times hysterical journey, I have triumphed. <br><br><a href="http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/Halloween%20Upload/GIFS/tumblr_inline_mnijcpINDA1qz4rgp_zps01e3a981.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396902888ra/9201014.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mnijcpINDA1qz4rgp_zps01e3a981.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It was exactly 3% that I realized the error of my ways. I like many of you awaited the publication of what I hoped to be Wards return to her former glory, reconnecting with the characters who started it all. With an omnipresent sense of dread I started The King, allowing my buoyant optimism to overshadow the fact that the last two books were a disastrous blunder. It was then, I read the following:<br><br><b><blockquote> He was the last purebred vampire left on the planet - and when it came to her and sex, he was fully capable of going wrecking-ball to get at her. <u> And not in the stupid-ass Miley Cyrus poser-sex way - and provided Beth was willing, of course. </u> </blockquote> </b><br><br><a href="http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/anigif_original-grid-image-26669-1390307678-3_zps6277e3f6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396665699ra/9170251.gif" alt=" photo anigif_original-grid-image-26669-1390307678-3_zps6277e3f6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><i> If this tickles your fancy, I encourage you to read through my status updates. Quotes of this caliber are in abundance. </i><br><br>This book, and I'm being generous even calling it that, is a far cry from what we all know her to be capable of. The sad part is, as a long standing BDB fan it truly is sad for me, that under all the bullshit is an actual story, one I know, love and miss dearly. This shouldn't be called The King, it should be called The Death Rattle of a Dying Series.<br><br><br><pre> <b> <u> Ingredients for The Death Rattle </u> </b> </pre><br>4 parts Miley Cyrus references (<i> added points with the mention of "twerking"</i>)<br>2 dashes of the word "defo" (<i> added points with the use of "abso" and "jel", use accordingly</i>)<br>9 mentions of the iPhone (<i> added points with the mention of Apple, Siri, or the opposer Blackberry</i>)<br>1 references to Facebook relationship updates (read: It's complicated)<br>1 nod to Nike's <i> Just Do It </i><br>117 uses of the word "sex"<br>2435 scenes featuring characters no one gives a fuck about<br>1 epic hose down of jizz<br>17 excerpts from fanfiction to save time<br>1 adult temper tantrum with the required use of tranquilizers<br>1 scene of the "good ole days" just to keep the reader hanging on, use sparingly, we don't want them getting any ideas here.<br><br><br><pre> <b> <u> Directions </u> </b> </pre><br><br>Take all your social references and sift together to remove any lumps. <br>Measure "sex" and pour in slowly, while mixing by hand.<br>Add "characters no one gives a fuck about" and "excerpts from fanfiction" fully incorporate.<br>Beat "epic hose down of jizz" until you have white fluffy peaks, fold into batter gently.<br>Grease your 9x10 pan with the softened adult tantrum.<br>Bake for 13 months at a low 250.<br>Let cool and garnish with 1 scene featuring past favorite characters<br><br>Plate and serve to your editor.<br><br>Suggestion: If you find that all those dated and unnecessary social references are bogging down the story flow, plow forward. You <i> definitely </i> need those, they are not jarring at all. <br><br><a href="http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/Halloween%20Upload/GIFS/tumblr_ma52qzVsRo1rvwttvo1_500_zps28267f03.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396908442ra/9202160.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_ma52qzVsRo1rvwttvo1_500_zps28267f03.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>So there we have it. Yet another disappointing and bizarre installment of the BDB. I will never do this to myself again.<br><br><a href="http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/Halloween%20Upload/GIFS/cover_tumblr_mf2vs7su4i1rccyxzo1_500_zps8dff0ae7.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396908243ra/9202118.gif" alt=" photo cover_tumblr_mf2vs7su4i1rccyxzo1_500_zps8dff0ae7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>BAHAHAHAHAHAHA. YEAH RIGHT.<br><br><br>Like a true dementia patient, I will read the next one. I will wait for it's publication. I will speculate on who will appear and what will happen. Perhaps a bit on my favorite brothers? I will get excited at the prospect of more time with Rehv or V. I will read every book of this series until she puts it to rest.<br><br><a href="http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/Halloween%20Upload/GIFS/anigif_enhanced-buzz-19430-1395679772-12_zps72d99d0a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396909638ra/9202331.gif" alt=" photo anigif_enhanced-buzz-19430-1395679772-12_zps72d99d0a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I know, I know, but it's because in those brief moments with some of my old favorites, I remembered so clearly how much I love these books, this world, and these characters. I've spent so much time in it that it all plays so clearly in my mind. The compound, their faces, their voices, the cheesy sex scenes, I love it all, and above all I am an optimist or some shit. <br><br>And so it begins again. <br><br><a href="http://www.ericapetiteame.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395070373i/8942755.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>

  <span id="freeText6901413553509120068" style="display:none"><b>PSA: Gifapalooza</b><br><br>My internal reactions a few pages into the prologue went something like this<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396452348ra/9135482.gif" width="280" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and this<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396452348i/9135483.jpg" width="280" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ward, you almost had me going there for a sec. Unfortunately, my feels didn't get much better as I read on.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396452348ra/9135484.gif" width="280" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was expecting the usual entertaining story, fun banter, cheesy lines, and a lot of kick-some-lesser-flatassery between the brothers.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396452348i/9135485.jpg" width="280" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Instead, I spent much of this 76 chapter book humming the theme song to <i>Scooby-Doo</i>, because the brothers of the <b>Black Dagger Brotherhood</b> were almost nonexistent.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396452348i/9135486.jpg" width="280" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm sad to say that I struggled to finish this book. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover at Last</a>, there were too many side characters with their own povs, and all of the side plots made for a frustrating read. <br><br>And what the hell is up with the name and brand dropping overload? It was fucking constant. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396452348i/9135487._SX540_.jpg" width="280" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396452348ra/9135488.gif" width="280" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I like getting to know more about the side characters and all, but why the long ass chapters of Assail and Sola interspersed with short, lame ass I-want-a-baby/I-don't-want-a-baby drama between Beth and Wrath?? Who is this book supposed to be about? And the baby drama was so predictable, it was boring. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396452348ra/9135489.gif" width="280" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396452348ra/9135490.gif" width="280" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In conclusion, all I have to ask the J.         <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25327841-p?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25327841-p?shelf=favorites-2014">favorites-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer898908992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10211893329997904409"><b>
  <blockquote>“Wrath - Beth x Overnight = Psycho-hose Beast”</blockquote>
</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481178775i/21394119._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='350' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was so pleased that I had a chance to read Wrath and Beth's story again. The King was my favorite book of 2014. Although I reread it again this year, I still insist this is as good as the first book of the series where all the stories begins. Wrath overcame his blindness and live happily ever after with his shellan, Beth, in the last books. Yet in The King, Wrath has to face a new challenge when his Beth wants to have a child, that's not easy </span>
  <span id="freeText10211893329997904409" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“Wrath - Beth x Overnight = Psycho-hose Beast”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481178775i/21394119._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was so pleased that I had a chance to read Wrath and Beth's story again. The King was my favorite book of 2014. Although I reread it again this year, I still insist this is as good as the first book of the series where all the stories begins. Wrath overcame his blindness and live happily ever after with his shellan, Beth, in the last books. Yet in The King, Wrath has to face a new challenge when his Beth wants to have a child, that's not easy for him because even she's a vampire, the risk is still too high, and he can't lose her.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1481178033ra/21394052.gif" width="400" height="180" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Rhage raised his hand " Pastor Ass-hat, I have a question." "Yes my son, you are going to hell”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I loved the dynamic Ward put in this book, she broke my beloved characters and made them stronger than ever by the problems in their lives. I liked many scenes from The King, especially <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[When Wrath shocks the shit out of everyone by showing them his son's pics. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> That was so heartwarming and the best moment of this book.<br><br>Besides, Wrath's parents are a suprising bonus; it shocked me how the two stories releated to each other and the past of his father still affected the present. J.R. Ward planned out this book so good I couldn't have asked for me. Every single page is full of dramas and twists that I grabbed the book very hard while something was happening and I knew that I couldn't stop it.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“By the power vested in me thanks to Google, I know pronounce you husband and wife! You may kiss the bride!”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481178775i/21394120._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/HPl1mv">https://goo.gl/HPl1mv</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_646022287" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/646022287" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/646022287?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">PNR readers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorite-or-autobuy-author">favorite-or-autobuy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=2014-cover-to-cover-challenge">2014-cover-to-cover-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=vampire">vampire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=owned-copy">owned-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=brotherhood">brotherhood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=antihero">antihero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=brothers-and-sisters">brothers-and-sisters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=animal-character-steals-the-show">animal-character-steals-the-show</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=found-family">found-family</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-or-heroine-blind">hero-or-heroine-blind</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646022287" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4485752176317062475"><b>I am not overstating to say that the release of the new Black Dagger Brotherhood series book is a highlight of my spring, and I view it as JR Ward's present to me for my birthday! That said, let's get to my review:<br/><br/><br/>**Disclaimer: This review is as spoiler-free as I could make it!</b><br/><br/>Wrath, Son of Wrath and Beth Randall have come a long way since <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42899.Dark_Lover__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___1_' title='Dark Lover (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #1) by J.R. Ward' rel='nofollow noopener'>Dark Lover</a>, and it's been my pleasure to accompany them on the ride!<br/><br/>When I first read Dark Lover (about eight years ago), I will be honest in saying that my b</span>
  <span id="freeText4485752176317062475" style="display:none"><b>I am not overstating to say that the release of the new Black Dagger Brotherhood series book is a highlight of my spring, and I view it as JR Ward's present to me for my birthday! That said, let's get to my review:<br /><br /><br />**Disclaimer: This review is as spoiler-free as I could make it!</b><br /><br />Wrath, Son of Wrath and Beth Randall have come a long way since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42899.Dark_Lover__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___1_" title="Dark Lover (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Lover</a>, and it's been my pleasure to accompany them on the ride!<br /><br />When I first read Dark Lover (about eight years ago), I will be honest in saying that my biggest draw was not Wrath or Beth, but the world and the storyline of the Black Dagger Brotherhood and the strange world within a world of Caldwell, New York. While I enjoyed their relationship, it didn’t blow me away, and neither character is my favorite in this series. However, I knew I was going to keep reading the series, and boy am I glad.<br /><br />With The King, I feel that an immensely important chapter has been closed in the Black Dagger Brotherhood, and it makes me happy because I feel that all the Brothers and their Shellans have found peace and the close bond of family, drawing close friends into their net. I also feel a sense of excitement in knowing that the storyline can continue and branch off in different ways and directions, and the waters seem uncharted. While there are tendrils that Ms. Ward has planted in this novel, I honestly don't feel I can predict too much about what is coming next. It's going to be fun to see where the story leads, and I am in no way ready for this series to end.<br /><br /><b>Character Thoughts</b>:<br /><br /><b>Wrath</b><br /><br />I feel we got to see some added depth to Wrath that was very good for expanding my view and appreciation of the King. He came to terms with some major hurts and issues he was facing, and I felt the flashbacks were a crucial aspect of the storyline. Wrath always regretted that he could not save his parents and he divorced himself from the concept of family and his legacy so long out of a sense of fear and guilt. In this book, he came to terms with his past and how his future did not have to be governed or hemmed in by fear. I loved his evolution as a King and what that responsibility came to mean for him. It was joyous for him to get everything he needed, but didn't even realize he wanted. Even though I know things didn't end well for his parents, their powerful love for each other and their son was still inspiring to me.<br /><br /><b>Beth</b><br /><br />Beth's storyline was thought-provoking. She was all over the place emotionally, and I understand why. I feel that she was at some of her deepest lows and her highest highs both in this book. While the story is about her, as Wrath's shellen, I think that more of the story was about Wrath. Her role seems more peripheral, but in a pivotal way. I still enjoyed reading about her character journey in this book. Beth is the best Queen for the race, and I can think of no other shellan to stand at Wrath's side.<br /><br /><b>Beth and John Matthew</b><br /><br />I think this book explored their relationship in a more satisfactory fashion than any of the proceeding books. They know they have each other's backs, and the readers as well. Also, it shows that although you may have your desired life partner, you also need the connection of family (blood and found). I almost thought the thing Ward said would never happen was going to happen, but it turns out that it wasn't necessary. I like the way the story unfolds instead. That John Matthew remains his own person, and his relationships with others aren’t hinged on his secret heritage.<br /><br /><b>Xcor</b><br /><br />Xcor remains a complicated male, not quite likable in many moments, and captivating and deeply sympathetic in others. Since I like my characters complex, he definitely has my interest, and he may turn out to be a new favorite of mine in this series. He remains a wild card in this new series arc, his behavior not the slightest bit predictable. To his great surprise, his feelings for a certain Chosen have opened closed off parts of his psyche, and this cannot be a bad thing at all. I think he will have a potential enemy in his own nest, but he’s not unaware of that. <br /><br /><b>Layla</b><br /><br />Layla is on shaky ground, but she is making her own choices and defining herself as a female. In her own way, she may have helped to avert a war that wasn’t going to end well, and that’s a good thing. I’m happy about that. I’m very excited to see where the story leads her next.<br /><br /><b>Assail and Sola</b><br /><br />Assail is probably the most amoral of the lead characters in this series to date. His behavior chilled me at times, but he was also very sweet in others to Sola and her grandmother. It’s hard to know what to make of him. I hope we see more of his viewpoint. I can’t believe their road ends here. Sola’s in a place where she has to deny the desires of the heart. How long will she be able to tune out the siren call of her unwise feelings for Assail, who logically seems like a ‘very bad man?'<br /><br /><b>The Shadows: Trez and iAm</b><br /><br />I am jubilant at the expansion of their storyline. These two promise to be a gamechanger in the series. We will finally explore the world of the s’Hisbe, and what a fascinating world it is. Trez has been running from his past for a long, long time, dragging his brother iAm along for the bumpy ride, as iAm has ever been his self-appointed guardian. iAm will soon step out of his brother’s shadow and find his own destiny, since Trez must soon face the music. Trez’s character is both repellant and alluring. He breaks my heart in many ways, but I feel hope for his future. I am drawn into this exploration of the dark path he has walked. The Shadows, once merely loyal allies of the Sympath King, have their own grand tale to be told.<br /><br /><b>Selena</b><br /><br />I didn’t expect her secret struggle at all. Another case of ‘keep reading’ to see how she will get her happy ending. And she had better!<br /><br /><b>The Usual Suspects</b><br /><br />It's always a pleasure to see the various characters who have had their books, and at the same time, I want more of them. I don't think the WARDen could ever sate my desire for enough of each character, honestly.<br /><br /><b>Overall Thoughts</b><br /><br />JR Ward, like every other author, has her own distinctive voice. There are aspects to her storytelling that turn off some readers. While I can see where she can overdo some of her affectations (like the brand name dropping and the copious use of slang), I love reading her writing. I feel that her depiction of the ancient culture of the vampires and their various subspecies is very poetic and dramatic, like an epic in its own way. Her romantic exposition lushly romantic and deeply sensual. It wraps around me like the dark spices her bonded males exude for their mates. Her tendency to adapt an urban vibe doesn’t bother me, because I think it’s an interesting juxtaposition to the very antiquated rituals of the vampires. While I can’t deny that the Black Dagger Brotherhood is at its heart a soap opera (not a bad thing in itself), it’s an enthralling one that draws me in and doesn’t let go of me until I read the last page (although the stories and characters continue to linger deep in the recesses of my imagination long after I finish the books). I feel like the Brothers, their shellans, and their friends/associations are part of my family, and each book release is like a yearly family reunion that I don’t dare miss. If only I was as excited to go to my real life family reunions!<br /><br />I’m sure that I could nitpick about the things I felt could have been better written, but I don’t want to. It won’t make me feel I wrote a better review, and I’m not sure it would change my rating at all. I just want to bask in the glow of a new release of one of my top three series. I don’t drink JR Ward Kool-Aid, but I certainly enjoy her fine literary comestibles. <br /><br />**The countdown has begun until next year’s release.**<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4485752176317062475" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText626437437314510554" style="display:none">January 15, 2018~ (Audiobook) Reread <br><br>It’s been awhile since I’ve read this, I was getting twitchy and needed a Wrath fix. I’m still completely and throughly devoted to Wrath!!<br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Smileys/heart_turn_love_zps68f9eb25.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416365ra/822194.gif" alt=" photo heart_turn_love_zps68f9eb25.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Smileys/heart_turn_love_zps68f9eb25.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416365ra/822194.gif" alt=" photo heart_turn_love_zps68f9eb25.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Smileys/smitten_zps82ef75c9-1_zps3c608306.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381820340ra/5325581.gif" alt=" photo smitten_zps82ef75c9-1_zps3c608306.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Smileys/heart_turn_love_zps68f9eb25.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416365ra/822194.gif" alt=" photo heart_turn_love_zps68f9eb25.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>5 Fantastic Royal Stars!!</i>
</b><br><br><br>We start this book with an introduction of Wrath’s parents, Wrath and Anha, I loved the insight into Wrath's parents. Their introduction, their mating, and the love they find and share. We also, learn of the incidents that turned the former docile King into a Warrior which we first learned about in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13570854.Lover_at_Last__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___11_" title="Lover at Last (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #11) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover at Last</a> (remember Wrath’s <b>
  <i>EPIC</i>
</b> speech to the Glymira, still gives me goose bumps!!) <br><br>In <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17703290.The_King__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood__12_" title="The King (Black Dagger Brotherhood #12) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">The King</a>, we get a clearer picture of Wrath, and the recent events that are responsible for him becoming a true King. In the last couple books Wrath has been growing more restless &amp; resentful of his role as King of the Race. He struggles between giving Beth what she <i>craves, needs, and really deserves</i> from him specifically a baby, his duty as King, and his desire to still be a Warrior. <br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/BDB/945F2727-8864-4345-9078-759A3071F7EC_zpstrqmp1ui.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1521518917i/25242128.jpg" alt=" photo 945F2727-8864-4345-9078-759A3071F7EC_zpstrqmp1ui.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As usual, we have multiple side stories. I loved reading more about the intriguing shadows <b>
  <i>Trez &amp; iAm</i>
</b>, the continuing story of <b>
  <i>Assail &amp; Marisol</i>
</b>, and <b>
  <i>Trez &amp; Solena</i>
</b>.<br><br>I am freaked out &amp; antsy about <b>
  <i>Xcor &amp; Layla</i>
</b>, seriously I have no clue how JR Ward will resolve their bond/relationship and the whole thing is making me nervous. I will say however, that I was a bit surprised that <b>
  <i>Xcor &amp; Layla</i>
</b> had managed to sneak a few meetings, considering how protective <b>
  <i>Q</i>
</b> was in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13570854.Lover_at_Last__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___11_" title="Lover at Last (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #11) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover at Last</a>...just how <i>did</i> she manage to slip away so often? <br><br>I have many favorite scenes, Beth’s needing being one of them….holy smokes I wanted to be Beth in that moment, Wrath can service me anytime, anywhere!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I can smell you,” he groaned against her ear as he ran his fangs up her throat. “The most beautiful thing in the world…except for your taste.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>But, I’ve got to say I freaking loved the wedding scene, Rhage, V, and Lassiter were hilarious.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Rhage raised his hand. “Pastor Ass-hat, I have a question.” Yes, my son, you ARE going the hell.” Lassiter made a sign of the cross and then looked around.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Wait, wait, wait.” V waved his hand rolled around. “I’m the son of a deity and she picked <i>you?<i>”</i></i></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>All in all I’m extremely satisfied with the direction the WARDen is taking with the series, and I’m definitely looking forward to much, much more BDB!!</span>

<div id="review_1370074076" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1370074076" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1370074076?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=fangywarriorteams">fangywarriorteams</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1370074076" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2305325953644628924"><b>Wrath, Beth and LW ( <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Little Wrath!  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>)</b><br/><br/>It is time for Wrath <br/><br/>1.	to fall in love again (And for us to fall in love with him again):<br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I can smell you,” he groaned against her ear as he ran his fangs up her throat. “The most beautiful thing in the world—except for your taste.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>2.	To renew his vows to Beth:<br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You have given me something ... I didn't even know I needed. It's the greatest gift I will ever receive--it's, like, completing me already in places I</blockquote></i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText2305325953644628924" style="display:none"><b>Wrath, Beth and LW ( <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Little Wrath!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>)</b><br /><br />It is time for Wrath <br /><br />1.	to fall in love again (And for us to fall in love with him again):<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I can smell you,” he groaned against her ear as he ran his fangs up her throat. “The most beautiful thing in the world—except for your taste.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />2.	To renew his vows to Beth:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You have given me something ... I didn't even know I needed. It's the greatest gift I will ever receive--it's, like, completing me already in places I wasn't aware were empty. And yet ... in spite of all that? I don't love you one bit more. You are as important to me as you've always been." He curled down and pressed a kiss to the loose shirt she was wearing—it was one of his, actually, and wasn't that great. "I was wholly bonded to you before this, and will be after this—and forevermore."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />3.	To become a father:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Before he knew what he was doing, he burst to his feet with Beth in his arms, leaned back, and hollered at the top of his lungs, with more pride than his six-foot-nine frame could hold.<br />“A soooooooooooooooooooooooooooooooooooooon! I’m having a soooooooooooooooooooooooon!”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />4.	To accept his responsibilities as a King.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Wrath rubbed his face. “They were good people, my parents.”<br />Abalone put the soda aside and shifted off the armchair, getting on his knees before his King. “I will serve you just as my father did, down to the bone and marrow.” <br />Abalone was dimly aware that others had filed into the room and were looking at him. He cared naught. History had come full circle … and he was prepared to carry forward with pride.<br />Wrath nodded once. “I’m making you my chief cleric. Right here and now. Saxton,” he barked out. “What do I need to do?”<br />A cultured voice answered smoothly, “You just did it all. I’ll draw up the paperwork.”<br />The King smiled and put out his palm. “You’re the first member of my court. Boom!”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />I guess this is the book that starts the second part of the BDB series: <br /><br />-It breaks the norm with the consistency of the books titles: Dark Lover, Lover Eternal, Lover Awakened etc. No more “lovers” in the titles from now on. I suppose we all know now that all the main characters are badasses and lovers. So there is no point repeating this.<br /><br />-It breaks the norm “one book, one HEA”. So far the books’ main focus was the main couple: Rhage and Mary, Vishous and Jane, Phury and Cormia etc. Now for the first time we revisit a couple that already had their HEA and we realize that there cannot be an HEA in this series for ever. Or maybe should I say better <u>all the couples that had happily ever afters so far, they need to be really worried because nothing lasts for ever.</u> And they all need to prove how much they love each other over and over again. (Ward laughs evilly here...)<br /><br />-More children are added in the series and now we can see the Brothers in the role of the father. Zsadist had a daughter already, but we will start from now on to see the interactions with other children as well and the Brothers will start talking to each other about children and ask advices. The series will be more family oriented from now on.<br /><br />-All the main characters have their HEA. Now the secondary characters will start trying to have their HEA and adopt a more central role in the life of the mansion. The mansion will be overcrowded from now on. Not that this is a bad thing.<br /><br />-There will be more interaction between <br /> a)the glymera and the king and <br /> b) the king and his subjects.<br />Vampires will start seeing their lives changing for the best.<br /><br />- Lessers will cause fewer problems (maybe the readers are tired by Omega and his lessers???) and the focus will be on the vampires and their problems.<br /><br /><u>This book brings Wrath again on a central role – in case anybody forgot that he is the number one, the top, the ruler and the ultimate KING.</u><br /><br /><b>Long live the King!</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2305325953644628924" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="MsMiz (Tina)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1679165-msmiz-tina"><img alt="MsMiz (Tina)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1309486634p2/1679165.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/576431148?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MsMiz (Tina)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MsMiz (Tina)" href="/user/show/1679165-msmiz-tina">MsMiz (Tina)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer576431148" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4924105186732151714">Mayhap this was the worst book in the series- well no - the desecration of Qhuinn and Blay's story sucked really bad. Ah shit, no Tohr's book was bad....god, have they all recently gotten bad and we are just glutton's for this stuff? Verily JR Ward has gotten ridiculous with the slang, hip hop references, and the uneven old world language. With alacrity this may be the last book I read in the series. Mayhap...not sure.....Okay I lied - I would read Lassiter, Murhder, I'am, I may even be happy ab</span>
  <span id="freeText4924105186732151714" style="display:none">Mayhap this was the worst book in the series- well no - the desecration of Qhuinn and Blay's story sucked really bad. Ah shit, no Tohr's book was bad....god, have they all recently gotten bad and we are just glutton's for this stuff? Verily JR Ward has gotten ridiculous with the slang, hip hop references, and the uneven old world language. With alacrity this may be the last book I read in the series. Mayhap...not sure.....Okay I lied - I would read Lassiter, Murhder, I'am, I may even be happy about Xcor's redemption...but we shall see. This was not the King's book - it is a running story of Trez, Xcor, Assail - all major asshats - a back story with The King's parents AND finally, a novella of the King thrown in. <br /><br />JR Ward has forgotten:<br /><br />1. The Brotherhood - where were they the majority of the story?<br />2. Editing - for god's sake woman, GET A FUCKING EDITOR! And if you have one, get a new one. <br />3. Loose threads - Honestly? The holes in this world are worse than the earth had with the Ozone. The rules have been stomped on so bad, it is hardly recognizable. <br /><br /><br />What worked - man oh man - Wrath and Beth. JR Ward did the King a disservice by including all that other bullshit in his story. It really took away from the real story. Wrath finding himself as King among the vampires, his brotherhood, and within his relationship with Beth. I will not spoil it, but lets just say, Wrath does not let us down not one second in this book. He will always be the one for me!!! <br /><br />The book was long, oh so long, yet the ending will feel like JR sucked on some Nitro and took off at 300 mph. What the hell, you give up at the end there JR? <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12133778320052026360">Review Posted on 4th April, 2014<br/>---------------------------------------<br/><b>4.2 "LONG LIVE THE KING" Stars</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>When you were without your husband, perfectly safe was relative.<br/></b>
</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396598740i/9157974.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Storyline:</b><br/>Multiple Characters POV's, So there's not just one tale to get along with. An extremely hard task to keep the spirit of book and JR did an amazing job with that, <br/>though it annoyed me sometimes.<br/><br/><b>Characters Development:</b><br/><b>
  <i>Wrath (King of Wrath I) & Anha </i>
</b><br/>flash back of Wrath's father's life, how he married to Anha and ruled </span>
  <span id="freeText12133778320052026360" style="display:none">Review Posted on 4th April, 2014<br>---------------------------------------<br><b>4.2 "LONG LIVE THE KING" Stars</b><br><br><i>
  <b>When you were without your husband, perfectly safe was relative.<br></b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396598740i/9157974.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Storyline:</b><br>Multiple Characters POV's, So there's not just one tale to get along with. An extremely hard task to keep the spirit of book and JR did an amazing job with that, <br>though it annoyed me sometimes.<br><br><b>Characters Development:</b><br><b>
  <i>Wrath (King of Wrath I) &amp; Anha </i>
</b><br>flash back of Wrath's father's life, how he married to Anha and ruled the vampire society.<br><i>
  <b>"He was King, yes. But first and foremost, he was the hellren of this magnificent female—and ahvenge her he would."</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b>Wrath (King of Wrath II) &amp; Beth</b>
</i><br>facing a turned of their lives that forced them to make decision eith of them is not ready to approve which gave us Royally Mad King and Queen full of dominant nuclear power. <br><i>
  <b>"When were you going to tell me?" Wrath demanded.<br>"Tell you what? That you can be a real a**hole? How about right now."</b>
</i><br><br>The Royal Couple had their moments but when it comes to stand by each others side so they can safe the race... they'll do anything they can no matter what.<br><i>
  <b>As he caught the scent of his leelan, all he thought of was that she was everything to him—and not just because she might well be saving his throne, right here and now.</b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392715470i/8599347.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>Assail &amp; Sola</b>
</i><br>Sola's the hot chic burglar Benloise setup to spy on Assail and been abducted in Lover at Last, Assail is on mission Saving His Marisol! and dear God! did he scared the ever living shit outa me which is beyond hotness.<br><i>
  <b>As good as this was, he didn’t need a weakness like her anywhere near his life. But like a wound filled with salt, she was permanently in his skin.</b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396598740i/9157975.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>Trez and Selena</b>
</i><br>Chosen Selena is the silver linning Trez didn't want to lose hold of but he won't allow himself to stake his claim because of s'Hisbe. I loved Selena the moment Trez first met in the last book and JRW made sure of keeping the charm of these two characters lively and steamy<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the way things are going with Selena it seems like fade is sniffing down her neck but still there's a lot more of Trez and her story which gives me a hope that soon we'll be having the full fledge tale of these two <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396532923i/9148126.jpg" width="320" height="290" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>iAm and Boo:</b>
</i><br>I know what you guys are thinking, character development with CAT?, believe me I was quite surprised too when I saw how iAm has hidden charms under his sleeves. His moment with GODDAMN were extremely hilarious, one moment he was Micheal Jacksonning over the silly cat and <br>next he was ordering around for proper food for his GODDAMN(BOO). In short, he practically adopted the cat. <br><br><b>
  <i>Début Character:</i>
</b><br><b>s'Ex</b>, an executioner’ came to warn Shadow and iAm about Queen's evil plans if Trez failed to complete the royal deed. s'Ex has so much intensity and power that I would love to learn more about character.<br><br>--------------------------------------------<br><b>
  <i>Lassiter</i>
</b><br>He'd simply stole the book! I have no words to express how much i love this stupid charming angel. (I want JRW to write a book solely on Leisster )<br><b>“Do you take this incredible woman who’s just saved your ass as your wife? Will you love and comfort her, honor and keep her in sickness and health, and forsaking all others, be faithful to her as long as you both shall live— crap, I was supposed to do you before him, Beth. How about you answer?”</b><br><br>-------------------------------------------<br>I like The King , if you'll ask me to rate it on scale 10 I'll give it 8.2 because this book was more about Assial than Wrath which disappoint me a little.<br>Anyway, back to our Royal Couple. Wrath and Bella are on odd trying to find a way to work out things with each other but having Wrath bull headed and determined on keepin` the love of his life safe and sound is making things more complicated. <br>I was pissed on Wrath for how he was treating Bella but I can totally understand from where he's coming. <br><br>As for the Old Century flash backs, <b>Wrath I</b> and <b>Anha</b> just melt my heart and made cry for the lose <b>Wrath II</b> faced at so young age.<br><br><b>FULL REVIEW TO COME</b><br>------------------------------------------<br><br><b>SPOILERS!!!!!!!!!</b><br><i>* Wrath and Beth trying for a baby! <br>* Saxton is part of a major future plot line.<br>* We will see more of Trez and Selena.<br>* Ward is working on Mary and Rhage's baby book as well.<br>* Quhinn and Blay will be mated, their story is not over. <br>* Lash will be back!<br>* She's working in Rhage and Mary's book. It's 146 pages as of right now. <br>* J.R. Ward is obsessed with Assail and his twin brothers are fucking awesome! <br>* Layla is 100% percent a Chosen fallen! <br>* Butch and De La Cruz will have a scene together.<br>* Xcor is going to have to make some serious decisions if he's going to be with Layla.<br>* The next Angel book is POSSESSION coming out October of this year.<br>* Butch will get another book.<br>* Payne and Blay will be brought into the BDB.<br>* Wrath and Xcor are NOT related, but ignored the question if Tohr and Xcor are related. <br>* We will see Layla's young soon.<br>* Havers will have nothing to do with Wrath and Beth's pregnancy. <br>* Sola is 100% human.<br>* The guy who was on the phone with Xcor is Saxton's father.<br>* Can't answer if Throe's family has been in the books....keep reading!<br>* Payne will be laying her hands on George at some point to restore his youth. Because the Warden is not having that "fucking dog die".<br>* Is Xcor going to turn on Bastards to get with Layla? "She is not going to be blowing his dick" unless something changes. "Keep reading"<br>* Ever do a book where 2 males bond to 1 female? "I ain't saying nothing about no shit there."<br>* Ward has to figure out the right time for Muhrder to come back to "do him" properly.<br>* Lassiter? You'll see him again. But when she brings him back, it opens up a section of his world. Needs time to do that.<br>* Lassiter - "Of course you are a Yankees fan you spineless son of a bitch" - Warden<br>* Beth's pregnancy could be shorter since she is a half-breed, more human. But Layla's is going to be looooong.<br>* Qhuinn's sister is really dead.</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1598876213?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1598876213" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3308960757982718723">I’ll be honest I was not looking forward to this one, it actually took me a year to finally pick it up and read it. Mainly because I desperately wanted a book for other characters and was disappointed this book was going to be about a character who already had <i>their story. </i><br/><br/>Well I was wrong, way wrong. I actually loved this one. I felt such a connection to Beth and was able to understand her desires. I felt like this story was so much more than the usual lesser slaying and loved how the story rea</span>
  <span id="freeText3308960757982718723" style="display:none">I’ll be honest I was not looking forward to this one, it actually took me a year to finally pick it up and read it. Mainly because I desperately wanted a book for other characters and was disappointed this book was going to be about a character who already had <i>their story. </i><br><br>Well I was wrong, way wrong. I actually loved this one. I felt such a connection to Beth and was able to understand her desires. I felt like this story was so much more than the usual lesser slaying and loved how the story really focused more on them as a couple. <br><br>This is actually one of my favorites in the later books. I felt like JR Ward really hit it out of the park on delivering a story that was emotional and heart felt, but still remained true to her BDB style. If you have taken a break I definitely recommend jumping back in! These last few books have really made me fall in love with the series again. <br><br><br>

<div id="review_575974168" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/575974168" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/575974168?book_show_action=true">Mar 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-paranormal-romance">genre-paranormal-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers">keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer575974168" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1049563597790141407"><a href='http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2014/04/review-the-king-by-j-r-ward.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333934i/693541.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Describe The King in three words</b><br/><br/>Angela: Satisfying. Emotional. Blissful.<br/><br/>Francesca: Sad. Emotional. Heart-warming.<br/><br/>Suzanne: I Love Wrath<br/><br/>Annie: LONG LIVE THE KING (Yeah yeah, I cheated.)<br/><br/><b>Did reality of The King live up to the hype?</b><br/><br/>Angela: Yes! He certainly proved his worth and then some. It’s not a surprise who the people will pick.<br/><br/>Francesca: It certainly did, and in a way that I was not expecting. But Ward is so great at that. This book was magical.<br/><br/>Suzanne: For me…yes it did, in fact it exceede</span>
  <span id="freeText1049563597790141407" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2014/04/review-the-king-by-j-r-ward.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333934i/693541.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Describe The King in three words</b><br><br>Angela: Satisfying. Emotional. Blissful.<br><br>Francesca: Sad. Emotional. Heart-warming.<br><br>Suzanne: I Love Wrath<br><br>Annie: LONG LIVE THE KING (Yeah yeah, I cheated.)<br><br><b>Did reality of The King live up to the hype?</b><br><br>Angela: Yes! He certainly proved his worth and then some. It’s not a surprise who the people will pick.<br><br>Francesca: It certainly did, and in a way that I was not expecting. But Ward is so great at that. This book was magical.<br><br>Suzanne: For me…yes it did, in fact it exceeded my expectations! I wasn’t sure what another look at Wrath and Beth was going to entail, would it just be a retelling of Dark Lover? Or them bickering over phantom problems? But it turned out to be much more intense than that and it made me fall in love again, not just with Wrath and Beth, but with the whole Brotherhood.<br><br>Annie: To be honest, I went into this book trying not to expect anything. I just wanted to be there for the ride. But Ward did something that not a lot of authors can do. She was able to take a couple who already had their HEA and give them something more. Something that not only added to the series as a whole, but also created some development in the character’s lives as well. Ward writes some of the most heartwrenching and touching moments you’ll ever read in romantic fiction.<br><br><b>How well does this fit in with the rest of the series?</b><br><br>Angela: I think with the turn of events as far as the throne goes, there will be a big shift in how this world interacts with each other. But Ward will have to bring on a big conflict, perhaps in the form of the Virgin Scribe or the Omega or even Lash.<br><br>Francesca: It’s crazy that I’m saying this, but this would’ve been a great ending to the series if just some loose ends were tied. I would’ve been satisfied with where this ended. Obviously the greedy reader in me wants more and I’m so happy that we will get more. But this book touched on most of our favorite characters, gave glimpses of the lives of many. And it certainly took their world by the balls. THE KING is definitely one of Ward’s best books as of late, I think, because she wasn’t afraid to go in a different direction. To make some major changes in the world. I’m so excited to see what’s to come.<br><br>Suzanne: I thought this fitted in really well, and not just fit in, but really stood out as one of the better books in the series. It ties up some story threads, whilst continuing others and open up whole new ones, keeping the series fresh, when I believe around Tohr’s book, it was feeling a little stale.<br><br>Annie: Well, the title doesn’t fit in at all. But despite my initial freak out, I found that THE KING really showcased the “bigger picture” of the BDB world. We see the glymera and their actions towards Wrath, we see Assail and Trez and iAm getting larger roles in the book. Xcor is stepping aside onto another path that I didn’t think we’d see from him, but together, it creates for a story that has its twists and turns while still keeping the several threads of romances going strong with each of the pages in this book. How THE KING is written sticks to Ward’s signature style so there’s much to love there.<br><br><b>There were different storylines and POVs in The King, which was your favourite, which was your least?</b><br><br>Angela: Well, Xcor and Trez spiked my interest equally. Both men are not so innocent in every sense of the word and they will be paired up with women who are completely opposite of their very being. I can’t wait to see them fall to their knees. But Assail is my fave. He is one hot, very hot hero.<br><br>Francesca: Obviously my favorite was Wrath and Beth, but aside from the main couple there are many I enjoyed John Matthew because I’m always a greedy whore for him, Saxton – because he’s a male of worth and I just need a full book about him and his HEA, and surprisingly iAm! I cannot wait to see more of iAm! My least favorite was Trez. If his storyline would’ve been wrapped up nicely in this book I would’ve been satisfied. I really have no interest in reading more about him.<br><br>Suzanne: I know there are some people who don’t like the different story lines that weave through the books and instead wants it all concentrated on the main couple. But I am not one of those people. I thought the balance of the Wrath and Beth vs the other characters was perfect, there was plenty of the main couple, we didn’t need to spend 90% of the book with them, especially when there were other interesting things happening. The characters story line I thought I would find tedious was Assail and Sola’s, as I hadn’t warmed up to Assail very much…I should have known that Ward would make me do a 180 and I instead found myself looking forward to their POVs. But the POV I found myself loving the most (apart from Wrath and Beth) was Trez and iAm, especially iAm, I canont wait to see what happens with them!<br><br>Annie: Obviously Wrath and Beth were my favorite to read about. Their scenes together are so emotional that it’s hard to stay detached from their characters. You definitely feel every ounce of emotion Ward puts in her books. I enjoyed Trez and iAm a lot as well. So by process of elimination, I’ll say that Sola and Assail were my least favorite. I do like Assail, but while I admire Sola’s courage and actions, there’s still a lot of questions surrounding her and her purpose in the series. Until I know more, I can take or leave Sola.<br><br><b>Wrath and Beth…what are you’re thoughts on them after this book?</b><br><br>Angela: I think we will continue to see their progress after this. There is life after happy-ever-after, after all. Just like Z with his girls, life is always a work in progress.<br><br>Francesca: I have many thoughts. First Wrath was a major DICK! I was so pissed at him for a while because I think he could’ve handled some things better. But ultimately, I fell in love with him in a way that I didn’t think would happen. Then Beth. She started off annoying me a bit with her moods. But once she took control, she showed me a new side of herself. I can honestly say I ended this book LOVING Beth. She’s strong, she took care of her man and what needed to be done. She fought for her man. And the two of them together? Well, just refer to the sentence a bit back where it says I’m in love. Yeah, they were beautiful together. Beautiful!<br><br>Suzanne: I have always had a crazy obsessive love for Wrath, which has now been tripled, but I now have a little girl crush on Beth. Simply put she was awesome, she had an inner strength and compassion that I couldn’t help but admire. And together, they were fantastic.<br><br>Annie: IN. LOVE. Really, could you ask for a more perfect ending than that? I cheered, I cried, I panicked and I laughed my freaking ass off too. Dark Lover is my most reread book of all time, but I’m thinking with some time, THE KING will also have many rereads in the future.<br><br><b>In general, love or hate this book?</b><br><br>Angela: I loved this book. Wrath is and will always be my TOP FAVOURITE HERO. I don’t think J. R. Ward could ever do wrong when it comes to THE KING.<br><br>Francesca: LOVE! Love, love love. And the main reason why? This book breathes new life into the series. It brings a new love for all the characters. It’ll be the book that will make you fall in love ALL OVER AGAIN with your favorites, and the ones you didn’t think were that special. It showed me why I love Ward’s writing, and how it’s the simple scenes and interactions, a small dialogue maybe, that have such impact on your feelings.<br><br>Suzanne: Love, love, love. I think this is one of the best books to come out the series, although it may not have the page devotion to the hot ‘n steamy like the previous books, what it has is a an intense and emotional love story, as well as the beginnings of a few others. It also has some interesting plot development and I can’t wait to see where the story will go from here. And all told in the unique and urban-poetic voice of J.R.Ward.<br><br>Annie: I want to caress my book. Does that suffice as an answer?<br><br><b>Who do you think will be next in the series?</b><br><br>Angela: I’m hoping it will be Assail but I have a feeling it will be Xcor. I think he has very strict ties to what happens next to the Brotherhood.<br><br>Francesca: Xcor and Layla. For me, that’s the only choice. The only one I want to accept.<br><br>Suzanne: I think either, Trez and Selena or Assail and Sola. I would love it to be Layla and Xcor or iAm and whatever lucky female he shacks up with, but I don’t think their stories are quite as well set up yet as Trez and Assail.<br><br>Annie: I know Francesca and Angela said Xcor. Suz is going for Trez or Assail, but I’m gonna go for a big, big stretch here and just say Lassiter. Because who honestly wouldn’t more of that Elvis scene? It was definitely the best part of the book!<br><br><b>Read my alternate review at<a href="http://freshfiction.com/review.php?id=42986" rel="nofollow noopener"> Fresh Fiction</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="1049563597790141407" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
