<div id="review_778644859" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/778644859" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/778644859?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780451417053" href="/book/show/18079730-the-king">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of the series</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=jr-ward-jessica-bird">jr-ward-jessica-bird</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2014_reads">2014_reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer778644859" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8160833352025727955">I think I've been saying (or thinking) this a lot about the last 5 or so books in the series--<i>"It wasn't my favorite, but I liked it a lot."</i><br/><br/>There's nothing that can compare (to me) to the first 5 or so books in this series--they were simply outstanding and sooo addicting. That's not to say that there weren't some pretty good books to follow--I remember loving Rehv's book (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5098079.Lover_Avenged__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___7_' title='Lover Avenged (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #7) by J.R. Ward' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lover Avenged</a> and loving the one with Payne and Manny (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8492319.Lover_Unleashed__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___9_' title='Lover Unleashed (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #9) by J.R. Ward' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lover Unleashed</a>), and Tohr's book (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10993282.Lover_Reborn__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___10_' title='Lover Reborn (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #10) by J.R. Ward' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lover Reborn</a>, and okay I loved JM's</span>
  <span id="freeText8160833352025727955" style="display:none">I think I've been saying (or thinking) this a lot about the last 5 or so books in the series--<i>"It wasn't my favorite, but I liked it a lot."</i><br><br>There's nothing that can compare (to me) to the first 5 or so books in this series--they were simply outstanding and sooo addicting. That's not to say that there weren't some pretty good books to follow--I remember loving Rehv's book (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5098079.Lover_Avenged__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___7_" title="Lover Avenged (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #7) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Avenged</a> and loving the one with Payne and Manny (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8492319.Lover_Unleashed__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___9_" title="Lover Unleashed (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #9) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Unleashed</a>), and Tohr's book (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10993282.Lover_Reborn__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___10_" title="Lover Reborn (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #10) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Reborn</a>, and okay I loved JM's book too (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7046495.Lover_Mine__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___8_" title="Lover Mine (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #8) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Mine</a>) but they're not books about the Brothers (except Tohr), so they're just a tiny step below. So even though this book was partly about Wrath, I didn't have unreasonable expectations going in. And, I was pleasantly surprised. Not knocked out, but very satisfied.<br><br>Highlights: ( possible <b>spoilers</b> ahead)<br><br>*Wrath and Beth are at odds. Beth wants a baby, Wrath does not. Wrath hates much of the details that go in to being a King, and has moments where he wouldn't care if he was toppled from the throne. Until he has his eyes opened (not literally, unfortunately) and sees a better way to rule...<br>Loved everything about this storyline. I thought we knew all about Beth and Wrath, but Ward has way more to tell.:)<br><br><i>Wrath...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr100/wrath7_zps95a0c01f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397505291i/9284707._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo wrath7_zps95a0c01f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Beth...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr101/bethbdb_zpsa55b0fba.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397505410i/9284725.jpg" alt=" photo bethbdb_zpsa55b0fba.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>*Drug dealing, cocaine sniffing Assail saves Sola from kidnappers, and they hook up. It's hot, it's exciting, but Marisol sees no future in it if Assail can't give up his lifestyle...<br>This storyline is far from over. Marisol may have moved far away, but Assail is constantly on her mind.<br>I'm really starting to get into this sexy couple...<br><br><i>Assail...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr102/assail_zps281c3287.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397505491i/9284735.png" alt=" photo assail_zps281c3287.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>*Trez is getting tired of nailing everything in a skirt and is doing everything he can think of to avoid his unwanted future. What he'd really like is a chance with the Chosen Selena (who really wants him until she finds out about his past). he makes a deal with the Queen's bodyguard that may buy him some time...<br>I haven't been too interested in Trez until now. His storyline is starting to intrigue me and I like him with Selena. But I am also interested to see the person he's been promised to and has never met.<br><br><i>Trez...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr103/trez_zps62218dea.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397505569i/9284737._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo trez_zps62218dea.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>*JM is having seizures and they're connected to his relationship with his "sister" Beth. Will they ever realize that he's Darius reincarnated?<br><br>*Xcor gives up his quest for the throne in order to be with Layla. How is this going to play out? I'm dying to find out! What will Qhuinn think of Layla with Xcor? What will everyone think? Could this possibly be a love match? I can't deny that Xcor intrigues me too...<br><br><i>Xcor...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/books/0c889a93-683d-4062-94c3-bbe1a78fd765_zpse5b723c6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380380251i/737109.jpg" alt=" photo 0c889a93-683d-4062-94c3-bbe1a78fd765_zpse5b723c6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>*iAm--I never gave you much thought but now I want to know more, more, more! I love your relationship with your brother, and I really liked how you were there for Beth. And your sexual history compared to your brother's? What?! I hope JR Ward rewards you with a nice juicy storyline!<br><br>*Wrath's parents love story--loved it! Loved how it compared and contrasted with Wrath and Beth's love story. Many similarities, but a lot of differences too. Nice bit of storytelling and beautiful connection between the King and the BDB.<br><br>With this book, I think Ward has wrapped up Beth and Wrath's story. A whole lot happens to them but they come out of it better than ever--and happy. And I didn't realize only 2 years have passed since they were married (2 years--really??)<br>Anyway, Wrath really comes into his own as a ruler and a husband in this story, and Beth proves herself a strong woman and his perfect queen. Love this couple.<br><br>The rest of the storylines are all left dangling, to be dealt with in the future. Some of these stories have been around for a couple of books, so I hope Ward completes at least one of them. Every time I start a new BDB book it takes me a little time to get reacquainted with the characters, so the first couple of chapters can get confusing. That's how it was with this book--a lot to remember at first, but then Ward's sure hand and storytelling skills kicked in and it was smooth sailing from then on. The book became unputdownable annnnnd had a really happy ending. Really happy.<br><br>If I could have one wish for this book it would be to see more of the "Brothers". In this book we mostly see JM and V and Doc Jane, and that is in small roles. The rest of the brothers either had 'cameos' or just a mention. I realize Ward can't include scenes with every Brother but I wouldn't mind reading 100 or more pages if she could give us an update on the Brothers and their shellans, true?<br><br>An entertaining read that should appeal to fans of the series and leaves you hungry for more? 4 stars, easy; maybe even 4 1/2</span>
  <a data-text-id="8160833352025727955" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_575703076" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/575703076" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/575703076?book_show_action=true">Mar 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer575703076" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15344236373570372792"> <br/><br/>So we all know this is "suppose to be" Beth and Wrath's book and about them wanting/having a baby and while it's certainly that, it's just so much more!<br/><br/>I have a love/hate relationship with JRW's writing and I think the deeper she gets in this series, the worse it is. In certain chapters, she was bouncing all over the place and it was a hot mess. <b>
  <i>But...</i>
</b>it also allows her to give us many more stories and I do love that. <br/><br/>However, it did take till about 20-30% for me to really get into the book</span>
  <span id="freeText15344236373570372792" style="display:none"> <br><br>So we all know this is "suppose to be" Beth and Wrath's book and about them wanting/having a baby and while it's certainly that, it's just so much more!<br><br>I have a love/hate relationship with JRW's writing and I think the deeper she gets in this series, the worse it is. In certain chapters, she was bouncing all over the place and it was a hot mess. <b>
  <i>But...</i>
</b>it also allows her to give us many more stories and I do love that. <br><br>However, it did take till about 20-30% for me to really get into the book and at 592 pages, that took a bit. But that's finally when ALL the stories started to really get a grip on you and get good. <br><br>This book is broken up into FOUR main couples:<br><br><b>
  <u>♥ Wrath &amp; Beth:</u>
</b> Naturally, I LOVED their story. To see Wrath come to terms with what happens was amazing but to see him come through for Beth...priceless. Even though I'm not very happy with how he treated her before, I loved seeing him come unglued in the billiards room! The one thing I didn't get was the whole conundrum with the needing...how could she even have one? <br><br>And I just love how they are there for each other as a couple. They just get each other...it's a wonderful thing. <br><br>The flashbacks to his Mom and Dad were interesting but I Loved, LOVED, loved the dream scenes.<br><br>And I just have to mention how JM was with Beth...it was amazing. I just would've loved to have had more of JM's thoughts. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439786986i/15884628.png" width="300" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><br><b>
  <u>♥ Assail &amp; Sola:</u>
</b><br><br>Wow...I really like these two. The intensity of their feelings are so incredible. I even love how the twins and Assail like Sola's grandma. I don't know where this is going but I'm so on board!<br><br><br><b>
  <u>♥ Trez &amp; Selena:</u>
</b><br><br>Dang, I had no clue what a manwhore Trez was and his sitch (LOL) is pretty FUBAR but...there is hope. And I love him and Selena together although it's crazy what's going on with her. <br><br>I cannot wait to get more of Trez and iAm in the next book! I don't know which one I'm more excited about...Trez finding his mate or iAm getting some! And LOL about iAm and the "goddamn cat". And oh yea, the crazy sex god, s'Ex...can't wait to hear more of his story!<br><br><br><b>
  <u>♥ Xcor &amp; Layla:</u>
</b><br><br>Ugh...Xcor - what can I say? I <i>just don't like him</i> and I don't care that he got all dressed up! <b>Too little, too late!</b> And the only thing that redeems Layla is what her reason is. <br><br>But the worse thing? What in the heck is going on with Throe? That was pretty scary and just creepy and I'm so disappointed! I had such high hopes for him but I would carry Mace too!<br><br><br>But never fear, <i>almost</i> everybody makes an appearance although some of them, they're only mentioned. Where in the heck is Mary though? She didn't get discussed AT ALL. I mean I was happy to get some funny moments with Rhage but nothing, nada, zilch about his mate. I'm just going to believe she's off looking for a baby to adopt. Insert *happy thoughts*<br><br>I did love all the resolutions especially what happened with the throne and the Council (Rehv busts me up!). Lassiter and his outfit was hilarious! The ending was amazing...how could it not be? LW's guards are the best! <br><br>Bonus points - hardly any talk of Lessers, thank goodness. Now just bring back Lash already!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396760340ra/9184042.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><b>
  <u>Recommendation:</u>
</b><br><br>You really can't miss this book if you want to continue on with series. There's just too many things going on that you would miss and of course, why would you want to miss the soft side of Wrath? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385019943ra/7046764.gif" width="300" height="050" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ “I am the King, you realize.” <br><br>“And I’m the daughter of a deity, motherfucker.”<br><i>(Best comeback ever!)</i><br><br>♥ "Wrath - Beth × Overnight = Psycho-hose Beast."<br><br>♥ "And hell, when she thought about it logically, getting True Love along with Happily Married and Hot Sex Life was already one hell of a trifecta."<br><br>♥ “Holy shit.” Rehv shook his head and muttered, “Now we know what the zombie apocalypse looks like.”<br><br>♥ “I’m not strong enough for this,” he whispered in her ear—like he didn’t want anyone to hear that coming out of his mouth. Ever. <br><br>Running her hands up his powerful back, she held him just as hard. “But I am.”<br><br>♥ "Out here, my love, he thought. What you have lost is out here."<br><br>♥ "Xhex wasn’t normally down for the sap, but she covered his hand with hers and brought his palm to her mouth. Kissing it, she murmured, “I know. I love you, too. Forever.”<br><br>♥ "Rhage raised his hand. “Pastor Ass-hat, I have a question.” <br><br>“Yes, my son, you <i>are</i> going to hell.”<br><br>♥ “Her eyes are right on you, and that smile of hers? Million bucks, my friend. Million fucking bucks.”<br><br>♥ “You have given me something … I didn’t even know I needed. It’s the greatest gift I will ever receive—it’s, like, completing me already in places I wasn’t aware were empty. And yet … in spite of all that? I don’t love you one bit more. You are as important to me as you’ve always been.”<br><br>♥ “That’s just about the best compliment anyone’s ever paid me.” <br><br>“I don’t know … I just feel like you’re the perfect man.” <br><br>“Now you’re making me blush.”<br><br>♥ "But that was what happened when an ordinary mortal … did something worthy of a superhero."<br><br>♥ “I’m going to give you everything I can,” Wrath said gruffly, glad no one else was around. “Anything you need, I shall provide. And I’m going to love you until my last dying breath.”</span>
  <a data-text-id="15344236373570372792" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer575811179" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2880550491566916069"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399754i/773926._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4.25 "All Hail The King" STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396749386i/9182244.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What a story. It was quite the long read with SO many things going on but I really enjoyed this one.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm sensing a new pattern with this series since the previous book. The books from now on will seem to no longer just be about the main characters they are suppose to be about, now we will be getting the story lines of so many others as well. I will admit that this was the reason I didn't love <i>Lover at Last</i> as I might have liked to. But in this one, I guess I </span>
  <span id="freeText2880550491566916069" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399754i/773926._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4.25 "All Hail The King" STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396749386i/9182244.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What a story. It was quite the long read with SO many things going on but I really enjoyed this one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm sensing a new pattern with this series since the previous book. The books from now on will seem to no longer just be about the main characters they are suppose to be about, now we will be getting the story lines of so many others as well. I will admit that this was the reason I didn't love <i>Lover at Last</i> as I might have liked to. But in this one, I guess I was expecting it. So, I ended up enjoying it a whole lot more.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396749386i/9182245.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I'll start with the main story line, which of course belongs to Wrath and Beth. I. LOVED. IT. It was SO great to see these characters again after all these years that have gone by. It was great to see how much they have grown and evolved as a couple. They go through disagreements that make them question their compatibility. I absolutely LOVED Wrath in this one. Sure, I didn't always agree with the way he handled things but by the end, I had a HUGE grin. I was that overjoyed for them. I even really liked Beth despite her stubbornness. I really liked that she wasn't a push over and stood up for herself. I like that she keeps Wrath on his toes. The ending of this book was so freaking fantastic. I just can't wait to see how everything that happen will change the future of the brotherhood. It was quite the turn of events but I'm hoping it will be positive for them all.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396749386i/9182246.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I was one of the few that actually <i>was</i> interested in Assail when I read, <i>Lover At Last</i>. Now, after reading more about Assail, who it a total anti-hero, I still want to know more about him. He is pretty smoking hot. He is looking for Sola, after she was kidnapped and does whatever he has to do until he finds her. I really enjoyed the chemistry between these two. I didn't really like how things left off between them, so, I'm hoping something awesome happens in the next book that will cause them to reunite.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396749386i/9182247.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I'm not going to lie, when I read the last book, I wasn't that big of a fan of Trez or iAm. But that completely changed with this book. Again, I really enjoyed the chemistry between Trez and Selena. Trez feels completely worthless of someone like Selena because of his man whore ways and the business he is in. Trez was freaking sexy but the shadow freaking frustrated me with how many times he left me hanging. Still, I loved him and wanted more. I loved that even though Selena is a chosen, she was bold and assertive. She surprised Trez with her quiet confidence and that's what I really liked about her. This story line also doesn't end in happy terms, so I can't wait to see what is in store for these two characters. I also want to say that I think I may be falling for iAm, Trez's brother. I seriously want him to find a GREAT woman of worth. I loved how he opened up to Beth and really HOPE he finds the woman he deserves really soon.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396749387i/9182248.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>While I wasn't a complete fan of Xcor's story line in the last book, I was still left somewhat intrigued. I loved how Xcor falls and loves Layla. But I am left rather confused as to what exactly Layla's feelings and thoughts are about Xcor. I know she's attracted to him but kind like him because he's the "enemy". But she is also afraid of him so I'm not sure where their story is going to be heading. Especially how everything will work out with Layla being pregnant with Quinn's child and all. There wasn't too much of their story in this one, so I'm looking forward to reading how it all plays out.<br><br><br>I enjoyed the book completely, but it wasn't perfect either. While I enjoyed everyone's POV's and story lines, I thought it was a bit overwhelming at times too. WAY too many things were going on for it all to be put in one book. I would have liked for this book to have had more of Wrath and Beth than sharing their book with the others. I think a great solution could have been a novella or short for the other pairs. That way we could actually focus on each couple separately rather than getting fragments. So, that was pretty much the only thing I didn't really like.<br><br><br>What I did like, was that we got some info on Wrath's parents. I loved their pov's from the past and how it all came to a full circle. That was just awesome. I really loved it! And I was left super happy with Wrath and Beth's ending. I loved that there were a few moments of funny banter--which I wish there would had been more of--between the brothers. I really missed these guys so much. Overall, I thought it was a really great read. And I CAN NOT wait for Trez and iAm's book next!!! So excited!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="2880550491566916069" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_576319395" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/576319395" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/576319395?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101602188" href="/book/show/17703290-the-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=buddy-read-with-books-n-buddies">buddy-read-with-books-n-buddies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=damaged-hero-heroine">damaged-hero-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=april-reads">april-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer576319395" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18051541887315890678">Where to begin with this one?? For starters, I will say that I was so looking forward to this book. I swear that once a year just is not enough for the BDB series. I was nervous about this book because my expectations were through the roof, and whenever I have high expectations; I am usually let down in some way. Unfortunately, in some ways I was let down; however the story certainly wasn't drastically bad. My biggest complaint was that I just didn't get enough of my wonderful origional brothers</span>
  <span id="freeText18051541887315890678" style="display:none">Where to begin with this one?? For starters, I will say that I was so looking forward to this book. I swear that once a year just is not enough for the BDB series. I was nervous about this book because my expectations were through the roof, and whenever I have high expectations; I am usually let down in some way. Unfortunately, in some ways I was let down; however the story certainly wasn't drastically bad. My biggest complaint was that I just didn't get enough of my wonderful origional brothers. In fact, most of this book was about couples that haven't been a part of the BDB clan from the beginning. This really disappointed me, as I was expecting that everything was going to come full circle, and there would be some closure on some major issues that have been stewing since very close to the beginning. <br /><br />In Book #12, we get the storyline for not only Wrath and Beth, but of the past King and Queen. This is Wrath's mom and dad, and we get flashbacks that fill in some blanks about their history and how they met. At first it is confusing about who JR Ward is writing about; but once I figured out that it was Wrath's parents then I settled into learning a bit about their past. Considering that this book is called "The King," we don't get a very big storyline with Wrath and Beth. I felt somewhat cheated about that; but I will say that the parts with them were very emotional and intense. This made up for the fact that I didn't get to see them much. When the pages were about them, I was captivated, and I fully embraced the magic that has always surrounded this couple.<br /><br />As far as the rest of the book goes, it is about a few other couples. The problem for me was that some of these couples I was never emotionally attached to in the first place. This made it so that the parts in the story that were about these characters, often became boring and flat out frustrating. There was Sola and Assail, who I will admit did grow on me. Then there was Treyz and his Chosen Selena. Yes, Xcor and Layla were a part of this story; but surprisingly enough not near as much as I thought they would be. This leads me to my next thought about this book.<br /><br />I was under the impression that this was the last BDB book in the series, and then JR Ward was moving on to write about the BOB's? Without me revealing any spoilers all I can say regarding this is there was no HEA's for these couples. Things were left hanging, which means there must be another book coming out? <br /><br />So now we have another year to wait for answers that we were hoping to get in this book. Let's hope that when the next book comes out, our curiousity will be fulfilled and that it will be a book that will hold our attention! I miss the days of the first six BDB books. Those books held true magic between the covers, and I find that the newer installments don't have the same spark. I still enjoy Ms. Ward's humor and writing style, I just wish there was more of it and less chaos. All in all, she must be doing something right though, as I still wait each year until I can catch a glimpse of my favorite Brothers again. For some reason, for me it feels like I am coming back home to my own family...and I wouldn't have it any other way! </span>
  <a data-text-id="18051541887315890678" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('emd13Ydbn7hLJx0CkWbP1fO7XR55m/IVrUnqD+IBhg9AQRwPPAVW0OwMqWNmk8UKJeS61rcWfHL2N6y+L0J0lQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3RQgGQso4vBiRWO563a00xD80RK2zgUqllnA4is+GmjnMknLsHYrmMVu19gcg74MxqM22nhDi03NJ4ZT5n3o8g==')})
  }
//]]>
